<span data-key="7143f7759ef94ff8aeb01e4dfa3c097e"><span data-offset-key="7143f7759ef94ff8aeb01e4dfa3c097e:0">Netlify CMS</span></span>

<span data-key="063413e16b274f3a85e89db08cfed72f"><span data-offset-key="063413e16b274f3a85e89db08cfed72f:0">Netlify CMS is the first CMS for the new age of Git-centric web development. It is completely build tool agnostic and works with storing structured content in Git. A CMS for site generators. Netlify CMS gives non-technical users a simple way to edit and add content to any site built with a site generator. </span></span><a href="https://www.netlifycms.org/" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="ec53cd160cd34d5198c1be70fe5b529d" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="c4bc1804961b4a37b70ed33c2497b566"><span data-offset-key="c4bc1804961b4a37b70ed33c2497b566:0">https://www.netlifycms.org</span></span></span></a><span data-key="a1eb50bad2b64125ba8726554075b2f1"><span data-offset-key="a1eb50bad2b64125ba8726554075b2f1:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>

<span data-key="7f977dbed0f7449f9e097ab346b976fd"><span data-offset-key="7f977dbed0f7449f9e097ab346b976fd:0">Google Cloud Client Library for Ruby</span></span>

<span data-key="9df7774e650140fdafa66fdb621199cf"><span data-offset-key="9df7774e650140fdafa66fdb621199cf:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://github.com/GoogleCloudPlatform/google-cloud-ruby" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="2038414d4bfa439c9c292e4e0ce162ac" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="60c05f4cdbf34a10b6ef68629973f4f2"><span data-offset-key="60c05f4cdbf34a10b6ef68629973f4f2:0">Contribute on GitHub</span></span></span></a><span data-key="a5038919a7ed41fe87afdd25cf8e0890"><span data-offset-key="a5038919a7ed41fe87afdd25cf8e0890:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>

### 

<span data-key="b2723b1ddacf4eaf95f7e6cf0d490bae"><span data-offset-key="b2723b1ddacf4eaf95f7e6cf0d490bae:0">Boulder</span></span>

<span data-key="258e84b01db14bfea6e58890887b7b01"><span data-offset-key="258e84b01db14bfea6e58890887b7b01:0">An ACME-based CA, written in Go. </span></span><a href="https://github.com/letsencrypt/boulder" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="531003969f2d4844b6975e875d0eaf88" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="200014348201465e8010b2dd158d58ba"><span data-offset-key="200014348201465e8010b2dd158d58ba:0">https://github.com/letsencrypt/boulder</span></span></span></a><span data-key="908ec7dd3c7f4c14b4273a4fdab064a0"><span data-offset-key="908ec7dd3c7f4c14b4273a4fdab064a0:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>

<span data-key="fc77e7f9a66b48c6859f320067e44209"><span data-offset-key="fc77e7f9a66b48c6859f320067e44209:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://github.com/letsencrypt/boulder" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="996bf8e0db4d472da47bc0f0f8f45e43" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="88005d6d83654ac7a28b42b2d47c9d9d"><span data-offset-key="88005d6d83654ac7a28b42b2d47c9d9d:0">Contribute on GitHub</span></span></span></a><span data-key="d93e471d2a1745d1a915bd8db7e7791c"><span data-offset-key="d93e471d2a1745d1a915bd8db7e7791c:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>

### 

<span data-key="d40dde62503f407aa09d11bf23a75931"><span data-offset-key="d40dde62503f407aa09d11bf23a75931:0">Lego</span></span>

<span data-key="5c2434551a2c4d09868c8a3f61ee1ced"><span data-offset-key="5c2434551a2c4d09868c8a3f61ee1ced:0">Let's Encrypt client and ACME library written in Go. </span></span><a href="https://github.com/xenolf/lego" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="94d93683376e43648a23c033075bdcc4" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="c0e2b8a5fa434ab7a2f73de6f9241b5b"><span data-offset-key="c0e2b8a5fa434ab7a2f73de6f9241b5b:0">https://github.com/xenolf/lego</span></span></span></a><span data-key="007a801f02af4595bc56a3327274249c"><span data-offset-key="007a801f02af4595bc56a3327274249c:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>

<span data-key="f6dde2cc8dc84d66b4bb321cc944b9f7"><span data-offset-key="f6dde2cc8dc84d66b4bb321cc944b9f7:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://github.com/xenolf/lego" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="0c6f9ab5147a4a49a5ec08ee8fa21cec" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="b9d1cf19cb964915ac0518d1366a5dad"><span data-offset-key="b9d1cf19cb964915ac0518d1366a5dad:0">Contribute on GitHub</span></span></span></a><span data-key="6f9881f17d2b4503b81f7ce4f735a983"><span data-offset-key="6f9881f17d2b4503b81f7ce4f735a983:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>

<span data-key="36672277601a4831a703f86a386035d0"><span data-offset-key="36672277601a4831a703f86a386035d0:0">Site deploys overview</span></span>

<span data-key="a909f37c3c5c4e4db18b3679d15dfc2c"><span data-offset-key="a909f37c3c5c4e4db18b3679d15dfc2c:0">Netlify enforces a strict concept of atomic deploys. If you’re used to uploading files with FTP, SSH, RSync or S3’s API, this is quite a different concept.</span></span>

<span data-key="68e1e0cfb8a5463a8d471a59af569ebe"><span data-offset-key="68e1e0cfb8a5463a8d471a59af569ebe:0">Instead of pushing individual files to Netlify, you always create a new deploy. Netlify will compare the new deploy with your existing deploy and determine which files have changed and need to be uploaded.</span></span>

<span data-key="e978cd3ada3d46c68f41cff5ef342746"><span data-offset-key="e978cd3ada3d46c68f41cff5ef342746:0">No changes go live on your site’s public URL before all changes have been uploaded. Once all the changes are ready, the new version of the site immediately goes live on the CDN.</span></span>

<span data-key="e643a08fba954c75803cdfdf4f8649a4"><span data-offset-key="e643a08fba954c75803cdfdf4f8649a4:0">This means deploys are atomic, and your site is never in an inconsistent state while you’re uploading a new deploy.</span></span>

<span data-key="84e8850778e045a0bed6539633e3d2ab"><span data-offset-key="84e8850778e045a0bed6539633e3d2ab:0">With FTP or S3 uploads, each file is just pushed live one after the other, so you can easily get into situations where a new HTML page is live before the supporting assets (images, scripts, CSS) have been uploaded. And if your connection cuts out in the middle of an upload, your site could get stuck in a broken state for a long time.</span></span>

<span data-key="7b296737c6684aab93286d509e74271c"><span data-offset-key="7b296737c6684aab93286d509e74271c:0">Atomic deploys guarantee that your site is always consistent.</span></span>

<span data-key="27e9082f66e7485082a5747489deaa8f"><span data-offset-key="27e9082f66e7485082a5747489deaa8f:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://docs.netlify.com/site-deploys/overview/#deploy-summary" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="8f62304e250d4b47b0468ede44061af4" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="75d37fb9cdbf42e4a8b652e2e64fc36b"><span data-offset-key="75d37fb9cdbf42e4a8b652e2e64fc36b:0">#</span></span></span></a><span data-key="9480a1195b634c01b6f8dfc5cfbb38c2"><span data-offset-key="9480a1195b634c01b6f8dfc5cfbb38c2:0">Deploy summary</span></span>

<span data-key="4417a40842cb4a6d8084225f54089cf9"><span data-offset-key="4417a40842cb4a6d8084225f54089cf9:0">You can find a deploy summary on the detail page of any successful deploy, right above the </span></span><a href="https://docs.netlify.com/site-deploys/overview/#deploy-log" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="f4a0befad9b84ef5a6b1cf70ce6b93ea" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="7649617e5f5d469cbe046659c7e5e1c2"><span data-offset-key="7649617e5f5d469cbe046659c7e5e1c2:0">deploy log</span></span></span></a><span data-key="9ccd4950bbf84ea4b21e46f5fbc8187c"><span data-offset-key="9ccd4950bbf84ea4b21e46f5fbc8187c:0">. It allows you to quickly identify your deploy status and refer to the details in the log based on different types of information.</span></span>

<span data-key="247852c5a2894256ab698a3a1f21a680"><span data-offset-key="247852c5a2894256ab698a3a1f21a680:0">This summary indicates how many files have been uploaded to our CDN. It also indicates the status of site </span></span><a href="https://docs.netlify.com/routing/headers/" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="3ca43140e84c459f82bbe5686467923b" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="62592421b37e48d9b5ca145ebe3c3fa8"><span data-offset-key="62592421b37e48d9b5ca145ebe3c3fa8:0">headers</span></span></span></a><span data-key="1c371a738cae4ad2a7a85c218e339992"><span data-offset-key="1c371a738cae4ad2a7a85c218e339992:0">, </span></span><a href="https://docs.netlify.com/routing/redirects/" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="9ab64ff3959f4a3187d053d8fa0e2fd9" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="7c284fc9e1ba4fa484fd92c3e276697a"><span data-offset-key="7c284fc9e1ba4fa484fd92c3e276697a:0">redirects</span></span></span></a><span data-key="f343ae89898747dca4c580a5503adf68"><span data-offset-key="f343ae89898747dca4c580a5503adf68:0">, and </span></span><a href="https://docs.netlify.com/edge-handlers/overview/" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="ad0bd67ebaa34adc80fab38681ecdba8" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="e2aac75907f5439bbfae507d8cb48fd2"><span data-offset-key="e2aac75907f5439bbfae507d8cb48fd2:0">Edge Handlers</span></span></span></a><span data-key="33f9101a011a4fa0b52fb3301dbc6e5c"><span data-offset-key="33f9101a011a4fa0b52fb3301dbc6e5c:0"> included in the deploy. It also indicates whether your site contains content served over insecure HTTP, known as </span></span><a href="https://developers.google.com/web/fundamentals/security/prevent-mixed-content/what-is-mixed-content" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="b953b94422a84b53b7a5875248003d45" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="7f50dfbfbb6b4a5ebe6a9bc1936a205c"><span data-offset-key="7f50dfbfbb6b4a5ebe6a9bc1936a205c:0">mixed content</span></span></span></a><span data-key="789bb7121aae40df8465df28ce83165c"><span data-offset-key="789bb7121aae40df8465df28ce83165c:0">.</span></span>

<span data-key="c96d7e5f07f64e4e9bf0af24ebd8f91a"><span data-offset-key="c96d7e5f07f64e4e9bf0af24ebd8f91a:0">When you have </span></span><a href="https://docs.netlify.com/site-deploys/overview/#branch-deploy-controls" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="7ebe1c6dabf34d9a80ebbc959c7990b5" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="41fe023f1fd746e08fa89e986464b294"><span data-offset-key="41fe023f1fd746e08fa89e986464b294:0">branch deploys</span></span></span></a><span data-key="51a3344fcc1b422182434716edf29c4c"><span data-offset-key="51a3344fcc1b422182434716edf29c4c:0"> enabled, the summary will inform you if the files to upload have already been uploaded by a previous deploy with the same commits. Netlify’s deployment infrastructure knows how to avoid uploading the same file twice, even between different deploys, so we get your changes ready without duplicating content. You can read more about how this works in this article about our </span></span><a href="https://medium.com/netlify/how-netlifys-deploying-and-routing-infrastructure-works-c90adbde3b8d" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="7e6e5a2916e2427595ea81e1d9ca66a8" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="1a0e3a5e695248d8b5e59feeb87039be"><span data-offset-key="1a0e3a5e695248d8b5e59feeb87039be:0">deploying and routing infrastructure</span></span></span></a><span data-key="c266ffb8045f4dee89d5be56d7de7b97"><span data-offset-key="c266ffb8045f4dee89d5be56d7de7b97:0">.</span></span>

<span data-key="c25f30d8d3f64ff482cc60f6806c54ac"><span data-offset-key="c25f30d8d3f64ff482cc60f6806c54ac:0">If the summary continually indicates that many more files were uploaded than you were expecting, your site may be taking longer to deploy than it needs to. Visit our Forums for a verified Support Guide on </span></span><a href="https://answers.netlify.com/t/common-issue-making-the-most-of-netlifys-cdn-cache/127" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="e5a064d5e9e94dd9ba89a090ad213b72" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="d3545ffcb4804c65850002cd1d3fa106"><span data-offset-key="d3545ffcb4804c65850002cd1d3fa106:0">making the most of Netlify’s CDN cache</span></span></span></a><span data-key="722a161460a14b81ac5addfe6c198587"><span data-offset-key="722a161460a14b81ac5addfe6c198587:0"> to learn about why this might be happening and get advice about what you can do to reduce the number of files uploaded each time in order to speed up your deploys.</span></span>

<span data-key="b4b9bebfe0214ee2a6528efa4ef3c052"><span data-offset-key="b4b9bebfe0214ee2a6528efa4ef3c052:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://docs.netlify.com/site-deploys/overview/#deploy-log" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="d43062fd836b4ab1a4cde231ccbac3f0" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="8b6ee4427fe24bd79754e857c93e62fa"><span data-offset-key="8b6ee4427fe24bd79754e857c93e62fa:0">#</span></span></span></a><span data-key="7488845f7e3b4216a2c7bc2cc9a65b1a"><span data-offset-key="7488845f7e3b4216a2c7bc2cc9a65b1a:0">Deploy log</span></span>

<span data-key="062ed61ad32742a0a459470eaa1fd5ef"><span data-offset-key="062ed61ad32742a0a459470eaa1fd5ef:0">You can find a deploy log on the detail page of every deploy. The log provides content such as:</span></span>

-   

    <span data-key="2436e5747cc148dbb2ab558ca5f1a6ee"><span data-offset-key="2436e5747cc148dbb2ab558ca5f1a6ee:0">details about your site’s build image, dependency caching, and Netlify Build process, including all of the standard output which comes from running your build</span></span>

-   

    <span data-key="9f15c6020ffe4b508c533c87e16356a4"><span data-offset-key="9f15c6020ffe4b508c533c87e16356a4:0">information about any Build Plugins your site may have installed and their execution</span></span>

-   

    <span data-key="86d10103b1d5413f9d5fbdf721506e98"><span data-offset-key="86d10103b1d5413f9d5fbdf721506e98:0">details about the success, failure, or cancellation of the deploy</span></span>

<span data-key="118691a2ccdf46c68b335fda28280b18"><span data-offset-key="118691a2ccdf46c68b335fda28280b18:0">For any successful deploy, highlights from the deploy log will be included in the </span></span><a href="https://docs.netlify.com/site-deploys/overview/#deploy-summary" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="9d16c2ef793748799c2423f8337a7735" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="fa1fd598b31b456abc35ed1c53c37a87"><span data-offset-key="fa1fd598b31b456abc35ed1c53c37a87:0">deploy summary</span></span></span></a><span data-key="1d0b067183ac4780a00e7ca7ff31fc07"><span data-offset-key="1d0b067183ac4780a00e7ca7ff31fc07:0">. For failed deploys, visit our Forums for a verified Support Guide on </span></span><a href="https://answers.netlify.com/t/common-issue-using-build-logs-to-debug-your-build-process/3067" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="e3bb2a4fdb304b52944a04a9579608ef" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="6b5fce59ff454a73aa7271d545c50c72"><span data-offset-key="6b5fce59ff454a73aa7271d545c50c72:0">using the log to debug your build process</span></span></span></a><span data-key="060defe0d7a14f87aa18964068e9d43a"><span data-offset-key="060defe0d7a14f87aa18964068e9d43a:0">.</span></span>

### 

<span data-key="41bf1d8652a140a2bdb47bf0c26092ab"><span data-offset-key="41bf1d8652a140a2bdb47bf0c26092ab:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://docs.netlify.com/site-deploys/overview/#share-log-content" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="a540f858c3ec4d87a627b092bc3bf7a6" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="ab2eb7a024ca4e59b1007b25918f44c3"><span data-offset-key="ab2eb7a024ca4e59b1007b25918f44c3:0">#</span></span></span></a><span data-key="bfb051dd4a4d47c2bfe550711b17d476"><span data-offset-key="bfb051dd4a4d47c2bfe550711b17d476:0">Share log content</span></span>

<span data-key="24d37d081d1e4c22bdb391029fcc94a1"><span data-offset-key="24d37d081d1e4c22bdb391029fcc94a1:0">Deploy logs for a site linked to a private repo are available to all site members. For a site linked to a public repo, you can control </span></span><a href="https://docs.netlify.com/configure-builds/get-started/#definitions-1" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="645813d2785548e7834fdc2ad11ca8ea" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="64d0826aaafa4c5f98842c98d521196f"><span data-offset-key="64d0826aaafa4c5f98842c98d521196f:0">deploy log visibility</span></span></span></a><span data-key="4c451ab36a2a473796853a39a3b79e74"><span data-offset-key="4c451ab36a2a473796853a39a3b79e74:0"> to determine the privacy level.</span></span>

<span data-key="9667c8b8dafe48d18d62abea8843270c"><span data-offset-key="9667c8b8dafe48d18d62abea8843270c:0">To share deploy log content, you can copy the entire log by selecting </span>**Copy to clipboard**<span data-offset-key="9667c8b8dafe48d18d62abea8843270c:2"> (the clipboard icon). You can also generate a shareable URL for a single log line or a range of lines.</span></span>

-   

    <span data-key="a64b2a36a05c4243a71644892f497e90"><span data-offset-key="a64b2a36a05c4243a71644892f497e90:0">For a single log line, select the line number to highlight the line.</span></span>

-   

    <span data-key="44ce1131dece46fd8854292943df0c1b"><span data-offset-key="44ce1131dece46fd8854292943df0c1b:0">For a range of log lines, select the line number for the first log line in the range, then press shift and select the final log line number to highlight the full range.</span></span>

    <span data-key="958e4fda2c274538915530c7ddf2dbab"><span data-offset-key="958e4fda2c274538915530c7ddf2dbab:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><span data-slate-void="true" data-key="cbd57935c9ac4e23828ae6947bf2c9c4"></span>

    <span data-key="f403384fc65d43d89b70d4a6d873315d"><span data-offset-key="f403384fc65d43d89b70d4a6d873315d:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>

-   

    <span data-key="eb4bc44640a64a9695bb30cb9a133e77"><span data-offset-key="eb4bc44640a64a9695bb30cb9a133e77:0">If needed, press esc to deselect log lines.</span></span>

<span data-key="108a5653dcab47cf8737b4bc3166a06f"><span data-offset-key="108a5653dcab47cf8737b4bc3166a06f:0">Once you’ve selected a line or range, copy the resulting URL from the address bar of your web browser. The URL syntax should resemble this: </span>`https://app.netlify.com/sites/SITE_NAME/deploys/DEPLOY_ID#L5-L10`</span>

<span data-key="ba94ee48e6d24d9580ed9b870be599d4"><span data-offset-key="ba94ee48e6d24d9580ed9b870be599d4:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://docs.netlify.com/site-deploys/overview/#branches-and-deploys" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="1a03db48a29443b7a3a9410d755fac58" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="7d35087720fd4fde89cec77a1a182a2f"><span data-offset-key="7d35087720fd4fde89cec77a1a182a2f:0">#</span></span></span></a><span data-key="6b9a57176bf74836971f4fec7acdd331"><span data-offset-key="6b9a57176bf74836971f4fec7acdd331:0">Branches and deploys</span></span>

<span data-key="c0e67b528f624c01b5e64724cd4a2e95"><span data-offset-key="c0e67b528f624c01b5e64724cd4a2e95:0">Netlify lets you control which branches in your Git repository you want to deploy.</span></span>

### 

<span data-key="991c21d4bc3c40299329cca2c9fc4c30"><span data-offset-key="991c21d4bc3c40299329cca2c9fc4c30:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://docs.netlify.com/site-deploys/overview/#definitions" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="05d483f8b1864f00b16a5a1c859204b7" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="b9b862af392b4a578b03478d861c6109"><span data-offset-key="b9b862af392b4a578b03478d861c6109:0">#</span></span></span></a><span data-key="5de3095a4ef4486591c5c8dd4a431ff3"><span data-offset-key="5de3095a4ef4486591c5c8dd4a431ff3:0">Definitions</span></span>

-   

    <span data-key="df7165e92a3e4f3393df2ad1de59804a">**Production branch**<span data-offset-key="df7165e92a3e4f3393df2ad1de59804a:1">: the Git branch that Netlify uses to build and deploy changes to your site’s main URL. For example, </span>`www.yourcustomdomain.com`<span data-offset-key="df7165e92a3e4f3393df2ad1de59804a:3"> and </span>`yoursitename.netlify.app`<span data-offset-key="df7165e92a3e4f3393df2ad1de59804a:5">.</span></span>

-   

    <span data-key="55e9e616e9674fa5b1012f8f35d50391">**Production deploy**<span data-offset-key="55e9e616e9674fa5b1012f8f35d50391:1">: a deploy from the production branch. If auto publishing is enabled, each new production deploy will update what is published at your site’s main URL.</span></span>

-   

    <span data-key="935131ad7f8b4feb8a913370a4bcca26">**Branch deploy**<span data-offset-key="935131ad7f8b4feb8a913370a4bcca26:1">: a deploy generated from a branch that is not your production branch. Branch deploys are published to a URL which includes the branch name as a prefix. For example, if a branch is called </span>`staging`<span data-offset-key="935131ad7f8b4feb8a913370a4bcca26:3">, it will deploy to </span>`staging--yoursitename.netlify.app`<span data-offset-key="935131ad7f8b4feb8a913370a4bcca26:5">. If you use Netlify DNS, you can enable branch subdomains, so the </span>`staging`<span data-offset-key="935131ad7f8b4feb8a913370a4bcca26:7"> branch example would deploy to </span>`staging.yourcustomdomain.com`<span data-offset-key="935131ad7f8b4feb8a913370a4bcca26:9">.</span></span>

-   

    <span data-key="c9af9e4065524819b9dcdcd277f6aabb">**Deploy Preview**<span data-offset-key="c9af9e4065524819b9dcdcd277f6aabb:1">: a deploy generated from a pull request or merge request, building the site as it would be if the proposed changes were merged. Deploy Previews are published to a URL which has the prefix </span>`deploy-preview`<span data-offset-key="c9af9e4065524819b9dcdcd277f6aabb:3"> followed by the identifier number of the pull request or merge request. For example, a Deploy Preview for pull/merge request \#42 will deploy to </span>`deploy-preview-42--yoursitename.netlify.app`<span data-offset-key="c9af9e4065524819b9dcdcd277f6aabb:5">. For more information, visit the docs on </span></span><a href="https://docs.netlify.com/site-deploys/deploy-previews/" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="2d6bd165e481486e968d854ee899f66e" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="d87cd65e691f4d7f92428500ec3fcc20"><span data-offset-key="d87cd65e691f4d7f92428500ec3fcc20:0">Deploy Previews</span></span></span></a><span data-key="ec23198dc6344d9c9d9610845701dec4"><span data-offset-key="ec23198dc6344d9c9d9610845701dec4:0">.</span></span>

-   

    <span data-key="059fce2db335477482711b083962a06a">**Permalink**<span data-offset-key="059fce2db335477482711b083962a06a:1">: every successful build of your site also creates a deploy permalink that starts with the deploy ID number. For example: </span>`1234abcd12acde000111cdef--yoursitename.netlify.app`<span data-offset-key="059fce2db335477482711b083962a06a:3">. The web content at this URL never changes. This is in contrast to production deploys, branch deploys, and Deploy Previews where the web content is updated when you merge or push new commits.</span></span>

### 

<span data-key="b16e190d266a463fa68988d9516ba8d4"><span data-offset-key="b16e190d266a463fa68988d9516ba8d4:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://docs.netlify.com/site-deploys/overview/#branch-deploy-controls" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="83a7f8a17f6d4563808ee5f9ced31a2e" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="df5a24ee5bf746b485f9b3410425e9b7"><span data-offset-key="df5a24ee5bf746b485f9b3410425e9b7:0">#</span></span></span></a><span data-key="4758143f3dc24e1b858cb3829183356b"><span data-offset-key="4758143f3dc24e1b858cb3829183356b:0">Branch deploy controls</span></span>

<span data-key="2124295dabfa4b57a55a79328737165b"><span data-offset-key="2124295dabfa4b57a55a79328737165b:0">By default, Netlify deploys the site’s production branch after every change.</span></span>

<span data-key="f151f8c82b134f4ea8c994d43463afed"><span data-offset-key="f151f8c82b134f4ea8c994d43463afed:0">To generate branch deploys for other branches in your repository, select your site on the </span>**Sites**<span data-offset-key="f151f8c82b134f4ea8c994d43463afed:2"> page. Then go to </span>**Site settings &gt; Build & deploy &gt; Continuous Deployment &gt; Branches**<span data-offset-key="f151f8c82b134f4ea8c994d43463afed:4">, and select </span>**Edit settings**<span data-offset-key="f151f8c82b134f4ea8c994d43463afed:6">. You can choose to deploy all branches (including future branches), or select individual branches you would like to deploy.</span></span>

<span data-key="24db51bcf38f4ab7b9f3c1e1dd92315c"><span data-offset-key="24db51bcf38f4ab7b9f3c1e1dd92315c:0">undefined</span></span>

<span data-key="395ff5e9b60d44a085358c59ebad5106"><span data-offset-key="395ff5e9b60d44a085358c59ebad5106:0">When selecting individual branches for deployment, type the name of each branch you want to deploy. You can also enter branch names you haven’t created yet.</span></span>

<span data-key="573f52530f634748ad29db6ad9850bd5"><span data-offset-key="573f52530f634748ad29db6ad9850bd5:0">Once you select some or all of your branches for branch deploys, Netlify will start watching those branches for new commits and pull/merge requests. As soon as you start pushing changes to those branches, you’ll find new deploys for those branches.</span></span>

### 

<span data-key="ac74f8ef303b4ceeafbc4b03751075a8"><span data-offset-key="ac74f8ef303b4ceeafbc4b03751075a8:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://docs.netlify.com/site-deploys/overview/#deploy-preview-controls" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="7bdf4a22660045b18ee6368a5a77f9e3" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="1379effa71484a2085d8d3338e78355c"><span data-offset-key="1379effa71484a2085d8d3338e78355c:0">#</span></span></span></a><span data-key="dd1a0acfa3fd41d1b1ca846076803383"><span data-offset-key="dd1a0acfa3fd41d1b1ca846076803383:0">Deploy Preview controls</span></span>

<span data-key="c3216ef3b5de4b69b9682ec8620a84f6"><span data-offset-key="c3216ef3b5de4b69b9682ec8620a84f6:0">By default, Netlify automatically builds Deploy Previews for GitHub pull requests and GitLab merge requests when the base/target branch is your production branch. If you enable branch deploys for some or all of your other branches, we’ll also build Deploy Previews for pull/merge requests against those branches. Collaboration tools available in the </span></span><a href="https://docs.netlify.com/site-deploys/deploy-previews/#collaborative-deploy-previews" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="72e68be0c343445e8b30e244be6c3281" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="78d0bcbb895c4be0bf823b9f41401ebc"><span data-offset-key="78d0bcbb895c4be0bf823b9f41401ebc:0">Netlify Drawer</span></span></span></a><span data-key="c7c79620ae4443108f562a9a8dcec876"><span data-offset-key="c7c79620ae4443108f562a9a8dcec876:0"> are enabled by default for Deploy Previews.</span></span>

<span data-key="255f558820af4231a0d1c200d68e7ed3"><span data-offset-key="255f558820af4231a0d1c200d68e7ed3:0">You can control in the UI whether or not Deploy Previews are generated for pull/merge requests. You can also enable or disable the Netlify Drawer. To change these settings, select your site and go to </span>**Site settings &gt; Build & deploy &gt; Continuous Deployment &gt; Deploy Previews**<span data-offset-key="255f558820af4231a0d1c200d68e7ed3:2">, then select </span>**Edit settings**<span data-offset-key="255f558820af4231a0d1c200d68e7ed3:4">.</span></span>

### 

<span data-key="f1bff1e4b3bf4c6a8c5e92920122ed1c"><span data-offset-key="f1bff1e4b3bf4c6a8c5e92920122ed1c:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://docs.netlify.com/site-deploys/overview/#search-engine-indexing" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="7e93717c9c6647a1a72402a665348193" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="421b7e6a354c45e290881ef116695be5"><span data-offset-key="421b7e6a354c45e290881ef116695be5:0">#</span></span></span></a><span data-key="cf826b791cea4212ba080032325d75c0"><span data-offset-key="cf826b791cea4212ba080032325d75c0:0">Search engine indexing</span></span>

<span data-key="f8ea66b37b0344f5b4b344cde55061f8"><span data-offset-key="f8ea66b37b0344f5b4b344cde55061f8:0">Netlify automatically ensures that only your currently published production deploy and most recent branch deploys can be indexed by search engines. Requests to Deploy Previews, unpublished production deploys, and old branch deploys will have an </span>`X-Robots-Tag: noindex`<span data-offset-key="f8ea66b37b0344f5b4b344cde55061f8:2"> header included in the response. Depending on how you use branch deploys, you may want to prevent even your most recent branch deploys from being indexed by search engines. You can do so by configuring </span></span><a href="https://docs.netlify.com/routing/headers/" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="6972a7bef94946069a0fcd21ba11b6be" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="c8aa1c7ecc184e529db7a56c90bca750"><span data-offset-key="c8aa1c7ecc184e529db7a56c90bca750:0">custom headers</span></span></span></a><span data-key="8568b28dfc464e94910bf2b4a8a38652"><span data-offset-key="8568b28dfc464e94910bf2b4a8a38652:0"> in your branch.</span></span>

<span data-key="b1ed5db353d74b6c82daafd4a7320cb2"><span data-offset-key="b1ed5db353d74b6c82daafd4a7320cb2:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://docs.netlify.com/site-deploys/overview/#deploy-contexts" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="61e3474ce25045d8976d9be88deb5f91" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="68aaf81f1349494e8e611f9d67924481"><span data-offset-key="68aaf81f1349494e8e611f9d67924481:0">#</span></span></span></a><span data-key="5ce36e0db04f4869bf42748aea40aa5a"><span data-offset-key="5ce36e0db04f4869bf42748aea40aa5a:0">Deploy contexts</span></span>

<span data-key="bd6b1a898cfe4d3b8b909d24b4f27cfe"><span data-offset-key="bd6b1a898cfe4d3b8b909d24b4f27cfe:0">Deploy contexts give you the flexibility to </span></span><a href="https://docs.netlify.com/configure-builds/file-based-configuration/" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="d76d8b2d595e48b7b5054674fecf3829" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="1339da5dc1e742568b90cbda6582ece2"><span data-offset-key="1339da5dc1e742568b90cbda6582ece2:0">configure your site’s builds</span></span></span></a><span data-key="a1b54d6c16144ae1b569ca566f45aa13"><span data-offset-key="a1b54d6c16144ae1b569ca566f45aa13:0"> depending on the context they are going to be deployed to.</span></span>

<span data-key="440375ab12e344909d175b7bec26cf1b"><span data-offset-key="440375ab12e344909d175b7bec26cf1b:0">There are three predefined deploy contexts:</span></span>

-   

    <span data-key="8c8e382324af4625b5867c726bfcb786">`production`<span data-offset-key="8c8e382324af4625b5867c726bfcb786:1">: this context corresponds to the main site’s deployment, attached to the Git branch you set when the site is created.</span></span>

-   

    <span data-key="df227717d83e401595f44d7314ea3187">`deploy-preview`<span data-offset-key="df227717d83e401595f44d7314ea3187:1">: this context corresponds to the previews we build for pull/merge requests.</span></span>

-   

    <span data-key="3e55456a6a084da0b069df3c0c059597">`branch-deploy`<span data-offset-key="3e55456a6a084da0b069df3c0c059597:1">: this context corresponds to deploys from branches that are not the site’s main production branch.</span></span>

<span data-key="2ed28194e190429c977193fd72d5bd4d"><span data-offset-key="2ed28194e190429c977193fd72d5bd4d:0">Besides these three predefined contexts, sites can use also branch names as custom deploy contexts. For example, a branch called </span>`staging`<span data-offset-key="2ed28194e190429c977193fd72d5bd4d:2"> will match a deploy context called </span>`staging`<span data-offset-key="2ed28194e190429c977193fd72d5bd4d:4">.</span></span>

<span data-key="29b0c742cbd2403d960fabd36eaebb69"><span data-offset-key="29b0c742cbd2403d960fabd36eaebb69:0">Deploy contexts allow you to override options from your site’s settings including the build command, the environment variables added to the build, </span></span><a href="https://docs.netlify.com/configure-builds/build-plugins/#configure-by-deploy-context" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="16f8f4ad4dcc47929227dcdae1cb0d64" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="3d841d7f89dd4af0af341a033a4eafcc"><span data-offset-key="3d841d7f89dd4af0af341a033a4eafcc:0">Build Plugin configuration</span></span></span></a><span data-key="ad184fb25aaa43c380432be094d302f0"><span data-offset-key="ad184fb25aaa43c380432be094d302f0:0">, and more.</span></span>

<span data-key="959249f231bc42bc8b77c785644d8389"><span data-offset-key="959249f231bc42bc8b77c785644d8389:0">Overrides are applied in a hierarchical order. The site’s global settings apply to each deploy, if we’re building the production site, and if you change options in your production context, they will be overridden. Only options that are set explicitly are overridden; if you leave one out, the build will use the value of the global settings or previous contexts. Environment variables are also overridden individually, for example, you can have access tokens as environment variables per context.</span></span>

<span data-key="fc749920ab134afaa3f9673c5cd2ed8c"><span data-offset-key="fc749920ab134afaa3f9673c5cd2ed8c:0">To configure deploy contexts, you must create a file called </span>`netlify.toml`<span data-offset-key="fc749920ab134afaa3f9673c5cd2ed8c:2"> in the root of your Git repository. There, you can set as many contexts as you want to configure.</span></span>

1

<span data-key="47dbf139f632401db4448b7206ade375"><span data-offset-key="47dbf139f632401db4448b7206ade375:0">\# Production context:</span></span>

2

<span data-key="102114d90937465091c78d8347348965"><span data-offset-key="102114d90937465091c78d8347348965:0">\# All deploys from the main repository branch</span></span>

3

<span data-key="624ec41a5090432ab802d6686d3027fb"><span data-offset-key="624ec41a5090432ab802d6686d3027fb:0">\# will inherit these settings.</span></span>

4

<span data-key="cc3e8b0ce4114923a4a4bbc759e1637a"><span data-offset-key="cc3e8b0ce4114923a4a4bbc759e1637a:0">\[context.production\]</span></span>

5

<span data-key="52fffed13d9947d89fdf9a7d986184ba"><span data-offset-key="52fffed13d9947d89fdf9a7d986184ba:0"> command = "make production"</span></span>

6

7

<span data-key="ea45209a675046c0a285b5505ff3530d"><span data-offset-key="ea45209a675046c0a285b5505ff3530d:0"> ACCESS\_TOKEN = "super secret"</span></span>

8

<span data-key="0b1b33c3efdc485c884e63ae4f830d57"><span data-offset-key="0b1b33c3efdc485c884e63ae4f830d57:0"> \# Deploys from main branch run this plugin in the build.</span></span>

9

<span data-key="e9aea4fb62a84b2198c7b6da0e7a4634"><span data-offset-key="e9aea4fb62a84b2198c7b6da0e7a4634:0"> \# Plugins context requires double brackets.</span></span>

10

<span data-key="17776a16dc5e4250a1e59e0eb7b8c0b4"><span data-offset-key="17776a16dc5e4250a1e59e0eb7b8c0b4:0"> \[\[context.production.plugins\]\]</span></span>

11

<span data-key="b4197d4a5890482b99ffdfec660179c6"><span data-offset-key="b4197d4a5890482b99ffdfec660179c6:0"> package = "@netlify/plugin-sitemap"</span></span>

12

<span data-key="ffb1ee21d5734845aa4e9cfc1cf03f7f"><span data-offset-key="ffb1ee21d5734845aa4e9cfc1cf03f7f:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="n">​</span></span></span>

15

<span data-key="2f27bf40d4f1433f99272f063fa87a86"><span data-offset-key="2f27bf40d4f1433f99272f063fa87a86:0">\# will inherit these settings.</span></span>

16

<span data-key="f648f0c3ac8a43b5a962d35d2bbee1bf"><span data-offset-key="f648f0c3ac8a43b5a962d35d2bbee1bf:0">\[context.deploy-preview.environment\]</span></span>

17

<span data-key="176078ede6824a18b055a4d6ea3e8eaa"><span data-offset-key="176078ede6824a18b055a4d6ea3e8eaa:0"> ACCESS\_TOKEN = "not so secret"</span></span>

18

<span data-key="5cb3de70edb34019ad61c64a3677423d"><span data-offset-key="5cb3de70edb34019ad61c64a3677423d:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="n">​</span></span></span>

<span data-key="5d52bbd3c7c64057b6764bba807c0f2b"><span data-offset-key="5d52bbd3c7c64057b6764bba807c0f2b:0">\# Branch deploy context:</span></span>

<span data-key="fbd74ceaf35e4dae82e9d1fdf909530f"><span data-offset-key="fbd74ceaf35e4dae82e9d1fdf909530f:0">\# All deploys that are not from a pull/merge request</span></span>

<span data-key="0f79fbc8a9984229aace51a2e6346af7"><span data-offset-key="0f79fbc8a9984229aace51a2e6346af7:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="n">​</span></span></span>

Copied!

<span data-key="642ec5cc8990418183f90bf9f7bb0c62"><span data-offset-key="642ec5cc8990418183f90bf9f7bb0c62:0">File-based configuration settings will override those set in the UI. In the </span>`netlify.toml`<span data-offset-key="642ec5cc8990418183f90bf9f7bb0c62:2"> file, settings for more specific contexts will override more general ones. For example, settings for a specific branch will override those for branch-deploy.</span></span>

<span data-key="b5dbc1e6f83742958adad1f4046fe516"><span data-offset-key="b5dbc1e6f83742958adad1f4046fe516:0">Visit our docs on </span></span><a href="https://docs.netlify.com/configure-builds/file-based-configuration/" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="ca018f285bdc483c9558c2e677fa1903" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="df75991002b8459b847abb87031f2cf2"><span data-offset-key="df75991002b8459b847abb87031f2cf2:0">file-based configuration</span></span></span></a><span data-key="775da3acccfb42cfb9eea3a8b850b5ea"><span data-offset-key="775da3acccfb42cfb9eea3a8b850b5ea:0"> to learn more about what you can do with deploy contexts.</span></span>

<span data-key="5dcc416196f84579ace3d430585ea15c"><span data-offset-key="5dcc416196f84579ace3d430585ea15c:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://docs.netlify.com/site-deploys/overview/#more-site-deploys-resources" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="97132dfed15e47328a75f547162922ac" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="9adb73764c314cfd8962e750f1513e72"><span data-offset-key="9adb73764c314cfd8962e750f1513e72:0">#</span></span></span></a><span data-key="144c48bc7de24e118ff1a6e1c00355e3"><span data-offset-key="144c48bc7de24e118ff1a6e1c00355e3:0">More site deploys resources</span></span>

    <span data-key="d3b826eaa32d404bbcf40e67cea73c57"><span data-offset-key="d3b826eaa32d404bbcf40e67cea73c57:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://docs.netlify.com/site-deploys/create-deploys/" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="ddb6bad75b264b9d92a7204848f24f79" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="ee5593417c5e4daf9c1045046c0feedc"><span data-offset-key="ee5593417c5e4daf9c1045046c0feedc:0">Create deploys</span></span></span></a><span data-key="ff3f3ae5cf3a4f97bd7ff9f92ebf038a"><span data-offset-key="ff3f3ae5cf3a4f97bd7ff9f92ebf038a:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>

    <span data-key="29f76292e248477a9a92d61c40ab4fb8"><span data-offset-key="29f76292e248477a9a92d61c40ab4fb8:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://docs.netlify.com/site-deploys/manage-deploys/" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="2c484e1734a149bebb19f9731568905c" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="90ae3f058d404235b4a62f1c83734533"><span data-offset-key="90ae3f058d404235b4a62f1c83734533:0">Manage deploys</span></span></span></a><span data-key="7411d40588f747fcbeb99ad45d6aa479"><span data-offset-key="7411d40588f747fcbeb99ad45d6aa479:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>

    <span data-key="994cd0d480fd407ab0ab2ab6219f5028"><span data-offset-key="994cd0d480fd407ab0ab2ab6219f5028:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://docs.netlify.com/site-deploys/deploy-previews/" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="3828cff195a44c6eaaaebf6b04dc3349" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="d296b4a148754067a47a9f50f5720719"><span data-offset-key="d296b4a148754067a47a9f50f5720719:0">Deploy Previews</span></span></span></a><span data-key="da983ba6127e41d39db5574a83b0fa17"><span data-offset-key="da983ba6127e41d39db5574a83b0fa17:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>

    <span data-key="7ca2b594729c4fa4a7ba2234c9d7ceed"><span data-offset-key="7ca2b594729c4fa4a7ba2234c9d7ceed:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://docs.netlify.com/site-deploys/split-testing/" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="0f4ae2476bf84310b236df5a57af3d46" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="4d30e47052f64ec0b3ab0dbdac12543d"><span data-offset-key="4d30e47052f64ec0b3ab0dbdac12543d:0">Split Testing</span></span></span></a><span data-key="db6cbacb55cc460a94526a452f2a231d"><span data-offset-key="db6cbacb55cc460a94526a452f2a231d:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>

    <span data-key="7d81b02fba3c4efe9a6fde181e6e57c7"><span data-offset-key="7d81b02fba3c4efe9a6fde181e6e57c7:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://docs.netlify.com/site-deploys/notifications/" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="a44a9c7536d94f3799fcfb2b0fa92bd3" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="408499b0587b457fb2293246675182a3"><span data-offset-key="408499b0587b457fb2293246675182a3:0">Deploy notifications</span></span></span></a><span data-key="74705e14b6d249aa829fb7d06eb9985e"><span data-offset-key="74705e14b6d249aa829fb7d06eb9985e:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>

    <span data-key="d841e0a745c54b3b93a58d9adc055871"><span data-offset-key="d841e0a745c54b3b93a58d9adc055871:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://docs.netlify.com/site-deploys/post-processing/" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="9f25a5c431cf452cb32688c61789fad2" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="b2fb420ba8d04cb29608e2a9c6e002e4"><span data-offset-key="b2fb420ba8d04cb29608e2a9c6e002e4:0">Post processing</span></span></span></a><span data-key="5bb9eef4995d4e81904050906b3c2267"><span data-offset-key="5bb9eef4995d4e81904050906b3c2267:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>

<span data-key="60fdaec8f34b46f19ed27308af42d032"><span data-offset-key="60fdaec8f34b46f19ed27308af42d032:0">Create deploys</span></span>

<span data-key="0378ddd76bab4dcaba69c09983c8e70f"><span data-offset-key="0378ddd76bab4dcaba69c09983c8e70f:0">This page covers features and tools you can use to create deploys with or without continuous deployment.</span></span>

<span data-key="e3f8d638c14840918b3a09b62f46a050"><span data-offset-key="e3f8d638c14840918b3a09b62f46a050:0">Note</span></span>

<span data-key="bb1b783ac4294d84a9fd9e188db7d83c"><span data-offset-key="bb1b783ac4294d84a9fd9e188db7d83c:0">When you create a deploy manually without continuous deployment, Netlify does not run a build command.</span></span>

<span data-key="8a83b24aac57424eb272e1be1cd5dcfe"><span data-offset-key="8a83b24aac57424eb272e1be1cd5dcfe:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://docs.netlify.com/site-deploys/create-deploys/#deploy-with-git" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="4373cc34e3704491b68aaca2d8e51fb1" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="5b02879ae7ab429ea0db8dbcbf64c315"><span data-offset-key="5b02879ae7ab429ea0db8dbcbf64c315:0">#</span></span></span></a><span data-key="be9f5a0b8b514d59a853aa8d447a32e3"><span data-offset-key="be9f5a0b8b514d59a853aa8d447a32e3:0">Deploy with Git</span></span>

<span data-key="d5e8e05b32eb492482f5b7e634f2030f"><span data-offset-key="d5e8e05b32eb492482f5b7e634f2030f:0">Continuous deployment works by </span></span><a href="https://docs.netlify.com/configure-builds/get-started/" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="87f8df31f554441eb47196571a66012a" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="f6eb94c581454c2189ee2ca0109eecaa"><span data-offset-key="f6eb94c581454c2189ee2ca0109eecaa:0">connecting a Git repository to a Netlify site</span></span></span></a><span data-key="e16c047cae0e486a8fac53decb4883a7"><span data-offset-key="e16c047cae0e486a8fac53decb4883a7:0"> and keeping the two in sync.</span></span>

<span data-key="7f1e2a32162d4d2ebd56672932972c9d"><span data-offset-key="7f1e2a32162d4d2ebd56672932972c9d:0">It works for plain static sites, but it’s even more powerful when you’re using a </span></span><a href="https://www.staticgen.com/" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="28103e44c07c4c259eed0dd8cf0fcf56" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="18ffc40eb65f4c8d96002006a9ca45b5"><span data-offset-key="18ffc40eb65f4c8d96002006a9ca45b5:0">static site generator</span></span></span></a><span data-key="f60242a818584e69a12db50bcd9a4ad1"><span data-offset-key="f60242a818584e69a12db50bcd9a4ad1:0"> or a frontend build tool like </span></span><a href="https://webpack.js.org/" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="348fce07cd3841cc94e2c83b7c891691" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="7f807518c2e84c4d9ff2aa0ec90262f8"><span data-offset-key="7f807518c2e84c4d9ff2aa0ec90262f8:0">webpack</span></span></span></a><span data-key="a3765591dab445748fb94e9fa37880a5"><span data-offset-key="a3765591dab445748fb94e9fa37880a5:0">, </span></span><a href="http://gulpjs.com/" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="63d5a97c83be423e9719fb877c10f3eb" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="5c3c0cd6a8034210ade4834e42dce72d"><span data-offset-key="5c3c0cd6a8034210ade4834e42dce72d:0">Gulp</span></span></span></a><span data-key="b140f252836b43e2a9bd7006d724e513"><span data-offset-key="b140f252836b43e2a9bd7006d724e513:0">, or </span></span><a href="http://gruntjs.com/" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="571d4b11aeec4cd2abc905f62c9ba15d" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="f11f4a51ba1e415caaad7f4437f6c166"><span data-offset-key="f11f4a51ba1e415caaad7f4437f6c166:0">Grunt</span></span></span></a><span data-key="272240bdf14d466b8365289718569e3f"><span data-offset-key="272240bdf14d466b8365289718569e3f:0">.</span></span>

<span data-key="54c28f5a279d421cb34043553c31439a"><span data-offset-key="54c28f5a279d421cb34043553c31439a:0">Netlify will run your build command and deploy the result whenever you push to your Git repo. The benefits of Netlify’s continuous deployment include:</span></span>

-   

    <span data-key="014460138e3a41a893b5c1c97db75e36"><span data-offset-key="014460138e3a41a893b5c1c97db75e36:0">No deploying without committing and pushing first</span></span>

-   

    <span data-key="29f3a8b79cd14fba88172ae45b5e6bee"><span data-offset-key="29f3a8b79cd14fba88172ae45b5e6bee:0">Easy collaboration through pull/merge requests</span></span>

-   

    <span data-key="c8f8ad82400f46868187f7b7482600bd"><span data-offset-key="c8f8ad82400f46868187f7b7482600bd:0">Fix a typo through your Git provider’s web UI from your mobile</span></span>

-   

    <span data-key="b02f34fdfb6b4d0689cab3e1562c0c1f"><span data-offset-key="b02f34fdfb6b4d0689cab3e1562c0c1f:0">Edit content without code by using a static site CMS, </span></span><a href="https://netlifycms.org/" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="b84faa4fad2041a6a553bf4b63812434" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="ba671c34d1ad4af6baf44483e65ee8ad"><span data-offset-key="ba671c34d1ad4af6baf44483e65ee8ad:0">Netlify CMS</span></span></span></a><span data-key="e035b0e5e69a401481d17efb9b68b846"><span data-offset-key="e035b0e5e69a401481d17efb9b68b846:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>

<span data-key="645b0576af794fe5b473cd7111eb9dea"><span data-offset-key="645b0576af794fe5b473cd7111eb9dea:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://docs.netlify.com/site-deploys/create-deploys/#netlify-cli" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="1301cd948e5f4e3bb9780549f0ed9e6e" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="f2ac97484a2447659f27cf86454a5ec7"><span data-offset-key="f2ac97484a2447659f27cf86454a5ec7:0">#</span></span></span></a><span data-key="ca5e10b543114863b2c5ab54f56f9ad7"><span data-offset-key="ca5e10b543114863b2c5ab54f56f9ad7:0">Netlify CLI</span></span>

<span data-key="f908483dcc91412e918f7918e7a88497"><span data-offset-key="f908483dcc91412e918f7918e7a88497:0">You can use the CLI to </span></span><a href="https://docs.netlify.com/cli/get-started/#continuous-deployment" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="8fec78f188c54781be198e36d857da5d" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="d040b91f36ff4411ab4f70eff64affe9"><span data-offset-key="d040b91f36ff4411ab4f70eff64affe9:0">set up continuous deployment</span></span></span></a><span data-key="bfca0e1d62714486be16b7e0575c604c"><span data-offset-key="bfca0e1d62714486be16b7e0575c604c:0"> for a Git repository. You can also use the CLI to </span></span><a href="https://docs.netlify.com/cli/get-started/#manual-deploys" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="2f2353c07a8842a690a26f79f8a32434" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="7769d365e8944f06a8c345306bc305fc"><span data-offset-key="7769d365e8944f06a8c345306bc305fc:0">create manual deploys</span></span></span></a><span data-key="8b5ce6426df9481e9456a615652e1564"><span data-offset-key="8b5ce6426df9481e9456a615652e1564:0"> without continuous deployment.</span></span>

<span data-key="291337ff93284ef3b853643575c4c6be"><span data-offset-key="291337ff93284ef3b853643575c4c6be:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://docs.netlify.com/site-deploys/create-deploys/#drag-and-drop" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="df9865748ff0415db2f75d569d348af5" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="16901ab9614c464db9a12aa08a3563ae"><span data-offset-key="16901ab9614c464db9a12aa08a3563ae:0">#</span></span></span></a><span data-key="aca16e94c5d947649f11739536609aba"><span data-offset-key="aca16e94c5d947649f11739536609aba:0">Drag and drop</span></span>

<span data-key="5df6212e21294e79862c75d63204cb82"><span data-offset-key="5df6212e21294e79862c75d63204cb82:0">You can create a new site by dragging a project folder to the deploy dropzone in </span></span><a href="https://app.netlify.com/drop" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="1ab887d58b0340bba166d38f118a2bc0" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="1130528193684d53b9aa90ae70677f38"><span data-offset-key="1130528193684d53b9aa90ae70677f38:0">Netlify Drop</span></span></span></a><span data-key="ce2521287caf4d5ea004dbff79e5563d"><span data-offset-key="ce2521287caf4d5ea004dbff79e5563d:0"> or at the bottom of </span>**Sites**<span data-offset-key="ce2521287caf4d5ea004dbff79e5563d:2">. If your site is not connected to a Git repository, you can deploy your site manually by using the deploy dropzone at the bottom of the </span>**Deploys**<span data-offset-key="ce2521287caf4d5ea004dbff79e5563d:4"> page. For teams without sites, a deploy dropzone will also appear in </span>**Team overview**<span data-offset-key="ce2521287caf4d5ea004dbff79e5563d:6">.</span></span>

<span data-key="efee559397294216ac11cdd501758232"><span data-offset-key="efee559397294216ac11cdd501758232:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://docs.netlify.com/site-deploys/create-deploys/#api-endpoints" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="b6f5140ffa7047a4976888fdac2f656c" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="88f2c63125ad4ab4ad48fe6cc2787190"><span data-offset-key="88f2c63125ad4ab4ad48fe6cc2787190:0">#</span></span></span></a><span data-key="35650c6bf0bb41cea9168f4cc4b8b005"><span data-offset-key="35650c6bf0bb41cea9168f4cc4b8b005:0">API endpoints</span></span>

<span data-key="6dcf0b4c5b3d4a838803ac43d620397c"><span data-offset-key="6dcf0b4c5b3d4a838803ac43d620397c:0">You can use the </span></span><a href="https://docs.netlify.com/api/get-started/#deploy-via-api" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="561ef297bbfb4a9fb7702e35d4e3aaec" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="a63002fce7ab44cb84c924c83b321d76"><span data-offset-key="a63002fce7ab44cb84c924c83b321d76:0">API</span></span></span></a><span data-key="d64318795aee486d87b8421e944f9fbb"><span data-offset-key="d64318795aee486d87b8421e944f9fbb:0"> to create deploys manually using a file digest or a zip file.</span></span>

<span data-key="b0b6d59a7d51467597038043c9fea898"><span data-offset-key="b0b6d59a7d51467597038043c9fea898:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://docs.netlify.com/site-deploys/create-deploys/#deploy-to-netlify-button" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="9c5c551b6d8e4387b46469ecda76f7e2" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="d079c981fe0340c580803205a57940fa"><span data-offset-key="d079c981fe0340c580803205a57940fa:0">#</span></span></span></a><span data-key="278889af5e1749c48bb0bf84ec564d65"><span data-offset-key="278889af5e1749c48bb0bf84ec564d65:0">Deploy to Netlify button</span></span>

<span data-key="29bebabdd4304d61b2ec2fb79d7dee34"><span data-offset-key="29bebabdd4304d61b2ec2fb79d7dee34:0">The </span>**Deploy to Netlify**<span data-offset-key="29bebabdd4304d61b2ec2fb79d7dee34:2"> button helps users deploy new sites from templates with one single click. It provides web developers a simple one-click step to let their users deploy those applications on Netlify.</span></span>

<span data-key="d52c4cdbfabd49a9bf290d0b4109f1c6"><span data-offset-key="d52c4cdbfabd49a9bf290d0b4109f1c6:0">It’s designed to be used in README files, documentation sites, and probably anything that renders as an html file.</span></span>

<span data-key="cb9dfa8a66a7465ca7362203ad5a9279"><span data-offset-key="cb9dfa8a66a7465ca7362203ad5a9279:0">This is an example of how it looks:</span></span><a href="https://app.netlify.com/start/deploy?repository=https://github.com/netlify/netlify-statuskit" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="afb6722f0ab64cf1ab8dcf0bff084e28" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="cbc8baed00e145dfbb97514741a7aefd"><span data-offset-key="cbc8baed00e145dfbb97514741a7aefd:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><span data-slate-void="true" data-key="9e950cb24dab4c82befa4148944fb43e"><span></span></span></span></a>

<span data-key="a7d32406e1864870b84dec4d77db0cf8"><span data-offset-key="a7d32406e1864870b84dec4d77db0cf8:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><span data-key="57210170602444f19c1dad51fdf9a89d"><span data-offset-key="57210170602444f19c1dad51fdf9a89d:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>

<span data-key="a77f0bf6ae9e4953b7f29ac732df7952"><span data-offset-key="a77f0bf6ae9e4953b7f29ac732df7952:0">The template code must be available in a public repository stored on GitHub.com or GitLab.com.</span></span>

### 

<span data-key="7453784914ca4aafa900c4f148dd6b1d"><span data-offset-key="7453784914ca4aafa900c4f148dd6b1d:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://docs.netlify.com/site-deploys/create-deploys/#markup" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="59a30043007745aea9983af3356f0dc1" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="1ce2bafa2afe471083eb34d20677cb3b"><span data-offset-key="1ce2bafa2afe471083eb34d20677cb3b:0">#</span></span></span></a><span data-key="07411ea677e24690938640204c4b517e"><span data-offset-key="07411ea677e24690938640204c4b517e:0">Markup</span></span>

<span data-key="aef2218ce61445858e3563618ab61436"><span data-offset-key="aef2218ce61445858e3563618ab61436:0">You can use any markup language that renders as HTML to display the button. There are two very important URLs that you’ll need:</span></span>

-   

    <span data-key="5ac0e1688ee74487afdcefc423ff3941"><span data-offset-key="5ac0e1688ee74487afdcefc423ff3941:0">The SVG URL for the button: </span>`https://www.netlify.com/img/deploy/button.svg`<span data-offset-key="5ac0e1688ee74487afdcefc423ff3941:2">.</span></span>

-   

    <span data-key="023992cecee548a19176c0a6727a0c0c"><span data-offset-key="023992cecee548a19176c0a6727a0c0c:0">The URL the button takes users to: </span>`https://app.netlify.com/start/deploy`<span data-offset-key="023992cecee548a19176c0a6727a0c0c:2">. This link requires the public Git repository as a parameter, for example:</span></span>

    1

    <span data-key="823a3adf6d164bf58bbc20210b8e7f3e"><span data-offset-key="823a3adf6d164bf58bbc20210b8e7f3e:0">https://app.netlify.com/start/deploy?repository=https://github.com/netlify/netlify-statuskit</span></span>

    Copied!

### 

<span data-key="ec3fba2cc591489fb6e1f50b6d7ac15c"><span data-offset-key="ec3fba2cc591489fb6e1f50b6d7ac15c:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://docs.netlify.com/site-deploys/create-deploys/#template-configuration" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="0d9dda3b384e4506a2fcc7e7dbc935c6" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="a26d69d3d6794f7a81aabe3bf20e7fdc"><span data-offset-key="a26d69d3d6794f7a81aabe3bf20e7fdc:0">#</span></span></span></a><span data-key="462b1488f4bd4feb8d4ff419674e2b5a"><span data-offset-key="462b1488f4bd4feb8d4ff419674e2b5a:0">Template configuration</span></span>

<span data-key="50c882a1ad934d27894b1ddb9cb13887"><span data-offset-key="50c882a1ad934d27894b1ddb9cb13887:0">You can provide a set of default values for your template directly in the template’s git repository. Create a </span>`netlify.toml`<span data-offset-key="50c882a1ad934d27894b1ddb9cb13887:2"> file in the root of the repository, if you don’t have it already. We’ll read the information from there. This file can also be used to set options for continuous deployment, you can read more about it in the </span></span><a href="https://docs.netlify.com/configure-builds/file-based-configuration/" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="6985507a430e4e6187bd92334d38f166" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="c3bb5430ea47425c92a5c5e4c439c4f5"><span data-offset-key="c3bb5430ea47425c92a5c5e4c439c4f5:0">file-based configuration documentation</span></span></span></a><span data-key="1f27a2386f874a21800f0b9b871cac14"><span data-offset-key="1f27a2386f874a21800f0b9b871cac14:0">.</span></span>

<span data-key="4489030cf5834303810ee897479b2b54"><span data-offset-key="4489030cf5834303810ee897479b2b54:0">Within the </span>`[template]`<span data-offset-key="4489030cf5834303810ee897479b2b54:2"> section in that file, you can set two directives:</span></span>

-   

    <span data-key="010aca6ffb044a5b98a6a9d23416ddbb"><span data-offset-key="010aca6ffb044a5b98a6a9d23416ddbb:0">A list of incoming hooks for the users site. This is very useful if you want to allow a third party service to control when to deploy the site. This is what headless CMS services like Contentful and DatoCMS do. Users can give those providers the address Netlify generates for their specific incoming requests.</span></span>

    1

    <span data-key="668970976b9f4fe8940a5f2cf1ee364a"><span data-offset-key="668970976b9f4fe8940a5f2cf1ee364a:0">\[template\]</span></span>

    2

    <span data-key="5fba8eee7ad8493ba818ab1c04b6641c"><span data-offset-key="5fba8eee7ad8493ba818ab1c04b6641c:0"> incoming-hooks = \["Contentful"\]</span></span>

    Copied!

-   

    <span data-key="c957e186d7464a0181a6bb925342eb64"><span data-offset-key="c957e186d7464a0181a6bb925342eb64:0">A list of required environment variables. This is the way to let users configure specific configuration options upon deployment. It also enables customization without having to change the code of the base template.</span></span>

    1

    <span data-key="ecda316006194fb28ae669d98a0c6b54"><span data-offset-key="ecda316006194fb28ae669d98a0c6b54:0">\[template.environment\]</span></span>

    2

    <span data-key="8ec704f96abc4c53920a0691f974dd52"><span data-offset-key="8ec704f96abc4c53920a0691f974dd52:0"> SECRET\_TOKEN = "change me for your secret token"</span></span>

    3

    <span data-key="652f63564a53461da75682f48d303557"><span data-offset-key="652f63564a53461da75682f48d303557:0"> CUSTOM\_LOGO = "set the url to your custom logo here"</span></span>

    Copied!

### 

<span data-key="55296f32eb2544b195747a06bd68af6d"><span data-offset-key="55296f32eb2544b195747a06bd68af6d:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://docs.netlify.com/site-deploys/create-deploys/#pre-fill-environment-variables" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="657f905d5df740f8b4d5c20981dc177a" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="30bbe9df08ff4ecaa1e191339d18738f"><span data-offset-key="30bbe9df08ff4ecaa1e191339d18738f:0">#</span></span></span></a><span data-key="c45be1eef4984cf1ad9636fcac959efc"><span data-offset-key="c45be1eef4984cf1ad9636fcac959efc:0">Pre-fill environment variables</span></span>

<span data-key="b29d448b0c6441f19e2455dd3c4c70f0"><span data-offset-key="b29d448b0c6441f19e2455dd3c4c70f0:0">You can pass environment variable values for the site template in the hash of the template’s Deploy to Netlify URL with key/value pairs. Using the example environment variables above, </span>`SECRET_TOKEN`<span data-offset-key="b29d448b0c6441f19e2455dd3c4c70f0:2"> and </span>`CUSTOM_LOGO`<span data-offset-key="b29d448b0c6441f19e2455dd3c4c70f0:4">, the resulting URL will be something like this:</span></span>

1

<span data-key="b59c127d4a0e44cba20614cbf0083aca"><span data-offset-key="b59c127d4a0e44cba20614cbf0083aca:0">https://app.netlify.com/start/deploy?repository=https://github.com/myworkspace/sweetkittentemplate\#SECRET\_TOKEN=specialuniquevalue&CUSTOM\_LOGO=https://placekitten.com/100/100</span></span>

Copied!

<span data-key="9cda77cfe8794fa1a21ea442a54e3b93"><span data-offset-key="9cda77cfe8794fa1a21ea442a54e3b93:0">Passing environment variable values in the hash ensures that they’re processed on the client side only. You can can create custom Deploy to Netlify buttons for your users with tokens and other secure data, and they won’t appear in Netlify logs.</span></span>

<span data-key="3ae57f84b5db4dc1b2de256c715f36b6"><span data-offset-key="3ae57f84b5db4dc1b2de256c715f36b6:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://docs.netlify.com/site-deploys/create-deploys/#build-hooks" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="942244ba84e0405dbb3cef2091b914b1" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="006e25fab3944417b04396a8c4c1d457"><span data-offset-key="006e25fab3944417b04396a8c4c1d457:0">#</span></span></span></a><span data-key="3b3a822d54644aacb51ef0e59b11ec49"><span data-offset-key="3b3a822d54644aacb51ef0e59b11ec49:0">Build hooks</span></span>

<span data-key="a5b2bac0aa8b446d954e7f3c03653e61"><span data-offset-key="a5b2bac0aa8b446d954e7f3c03653e61:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://docs.netlify.com/configure-builds/build-hooks/" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="f0a912084eb6440bb9fb7d5b66dd6869" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="a4131f3744874105be259c85fc1f72fd"><span data-offset-key="a4131f3744874105be259c85fc1f72fd:0">Build hooks</span></span></span></a><span data-key="e7915b79415b4f0e89f903fbd1e880c8"><span data-offset-key="e7915b79415b4f0e89f903fbd1e880c8:0"> give you unique URLs you can use to trigger new builds and deploys.</span></span>

<span data-key="f82b195c4032448cb04337e74cbad664"><span data-offset-key="f82b195c4032448cb04337e74cbad664:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://docs.netlify.com/site-deploys/create-deploys/#zapier-integrations" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="942df837022f4a0e9cf3918687281026" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="68dfb97e7aa14ca2a1da11316b58a0e5"><span data-offset-key="68dfb97e7aa14ca2a1da11316b58a0e5:0">#</span></span></span></a><span data-key="47cb1dd392674b088878776c6e953cb0"><span data-offset-key="47cb1dd392674b088878776c6e953cb0:0">Zapier integrations</span></span>

<span data-key="9f345aa6c4a949409aa2c71c34894e95"><span data-offset-key="9f345aa6c4a949409aa2c71c34894e95:0">Netlify is available on Zapier, where you can connect Netlify with over 1,000 other applications. You can use Zapier “Zaps” to start a new deploy of your site in response to a trigger from another service. You can </span></span><a href="https://www.netlify.com/blog/2018/11/07/automate-your-netlify-sites-with-zapier/" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="35e743a505b7473da3b9dfe3adac2aa0" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="81766de038ef44e8927776f86c2efc7d"><span data-offset-key="81766de038ef44e8927776f86c2efc7d:0">find out more on our blog</span></span></span></a><span data-key="8563b0044ed84292a634556c87380f0e"><span data-offset-key="8563b0044ed84292a634556c87380f0e:0">, or use one of the templates below to get started:Start deploys of Netlify sites daily</span></span><a href="https://zapier.com/apps/netlify/integrations/schedule/29330/start-deploys-of-netlify-sites-daily" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="40e2d0ed0045411f93b9bc728fa41a19" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="9cc96c4e8a7848bdad3d9f5a7c6785f5"><span data-offset-key="9cc96c4e8a7848bdad3d9f5a7c6785f5:0">Use this Zap</span></span></span></a><span data-key="d9320bcf5e4d410db43b2fd660409e95"><span data-offset-key="d9320bcf5e4d410db43b2fd660409e95:0">Start Netlify deploys when you send new Tweets</span></span><a href="https://zapier.com/apps/netlify/integrations/twitter/29745/start-netlify-deploys-when-you-send-new-tweets" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="1c276cde0932495486acc92f18765ac1" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="fbb02b8cfa5042ba875ec134ea04cf2e"><span data-offset-key="fbb02b8cfa5042ba875ec134ea04cf2e:0">Use this Zap</span></span></span></a><span data-key="a47680f3b3ab42af8a85ed0a823eeda1"><span data-offset-key="a47680f3b3ab42af8a85ed0a823eeda1:0">Start Netlify site deploys with the push of a Flic button</span></span><a href="https://zapier.com/apps/flic/integrations/netlify/29780/start-netlify-site-deploys-with-the-push-of-a-flic-button" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="91a6fa693b2f4c508755cc5bb0d8912d" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="b54a8168faa34982b0b525a16800199e"><span data-offset-key="b54a8168faa34982b0b525a16800199e:0">Use this Zap</span></span></span></a><span data-key="36795da463614b2bbe4689a34eed1119"><span data-offset-key="36795da463614b2bbe4689a34eed1119:0">See more </span></span><a href="https://zapier.com/apps/netlify/integrations" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="f979a33b66704ba5a5a7bb6ef1016ebc" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="5577c002d6d64ba7b6147a1a4cbc1b27"><span data-offset-key="5577c002d6d64ba7b6147a1a4cbc1b27:0">Netlify</span></span></span></a><span data-key="92f9271fade648a1876fc6faf2b29cbb"><span data-offset-key="92f9271fade648a1876fc6faf2b29cbb:0"> integrations powered by</span></span><span data-slate-void="true" data-key="0317c4c750e140e882195be960ea8224"></span>

<span data-key="8954ef7f57f749df906d6014bb9abb49"><span data-offset-key="8954ef7f57f749df906d6014bb9abb49:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>

### 

<span data-key="e0363f174ca84372b695133b36e8f8ae"><span data-offset-key="e0363f174ca84372b695133b36e8f8ae:0">Did you find this doc useful?</span></span>

<span data-key="0bc076be90a24bb6abf2b33db6705171"><span data-offset-key="0bc076be90a24bb6abf2b33db6705171:0">Deploy Previews</span></span>

<span data-key="76bb4ebc5fc8447781e5cb23a1a981da"><span data-offset-key="76bb4ebc5fc8447781e5cb23a1a981da:0">Deploy Previews allow you and your team to experience changes to any part of your site without having to publish them to production.</span></span>

<span data-key="a5c3d57593dc4a07b7a5cffd5029141a"><span data-offset-key="a5c3d57593dc4a07b7a5cffd5029141a:0">Netlify builds Deploy Previews by default for GitHub pull requests and GitLab merge requests. You can control whether or not Deploy Previews are generated for pull/merge requests. For more information, visit the </span></span><a href="https://docs.netlify.com/site-deploys/overview/#deploy-preview-controls" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="85a778229f674a0695ab6a848199f85d" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="02e22f4b3e754899b570698911273842"><span data-offset-key="02e22f4b3e754899b570698911273842:0">Deploy Preview controls</span></span></span></a><span data-key="b35a0c81e14446d595bf9727cff9bff1"><span data-offset-key="b35a0c81e14446d595bf9727cff9bff1:0"> docs.</span></span>

<span data-key="5d11c8d119a04dfa9bf26cd267bb4f51"><span data-offset-key="5d11c8d119a04dfa9bf26cd267bb4f51:0">For successful deploys, your pull/merge request comments include a link to the Deploy Preview by default. You can add, remove, or edit these notifications. Visit the </span></span><a href="https://docs.netlify.com/site-deploys/notifications/" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="70a35a758ea04aecadf09326b7305b86" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="b2c984901c4448d9a6ae9c5834cb1038"><span data-offset-key="b2c984901c4448d9a6ae9c5834cb1038:0">deploy notifications</span></span></span></a><span data-key="50748e81dcae4f3c88af791a38cda146"><span data-offset-key="50748e81dcae4f3c88af791a38cda146:0"> doc for more information.</span></span>

<span data-key="3db1ecc802cb4a84a6ffe5c0334fee9c"><span data-offset-key="3db1ecc802cb4a84a6ffe5c0334fee9c:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://docs.netlify.com/site-deploys/deploy-previews/#deploy-preview-urls" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="0a57ece3b533491a8ffad96f8d3e4161" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="b984ba3481564f02afa6603e001f7aff"><span data-offset-key="b984ba3481564f02afa6603e001f7aff:0">#</span></span></span></a><span data-key="34d785db58fc4c93aa20f2063724ac3f"><span data-offset-key="34d785db58fc4c93aa20f2063724ac3f:0">Deploy Preview URLs</span></span>

<span data-key="8bcbea3ed8b44d118be0d8685d6893a7"><span data-offset-key="8bcbea3ed8b44d118be0d8685d6893a7:0">Deploy Previews work by deploying pull/merge requests to a unique URL different from the one your production site uses. This URL has the prefix </span>`deploy-preview`<span data-offset-key="8bcbea3ed8b44d118be0d8685d6893a7:2"> followed by the identifier number of the pull request or merge request. For example, a Deploy Preview for pull/merge request \#42 will deploy to </span>`deploy-preview-42--yoursitename.netlify.app`<span data-offset-key="8bcbea3ed8b44d118be0d8685d6893a7:4">. The web content of this URL is updated every time changes are pushed to the associated pull/merge request.</span></span>

<span data-key="76816b4d26b1442d977c2827a3040c83"><span data-offset-key="76816b4d26b1442d977c2827a3040c83:0">You can share this URL with your team to collaborate and </span></span><a href="https://docs.netlify.com/site-deploys/deploy-previews/#get-feedback" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="f23d469e2e43470b86e328dfafbcf3a4" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="a3b20c64a3e647769a4515f6c307769d"><span data-offset-key="a3b20c64a3e647769a4515f6c307769d:0">gather feedback</span></span></span></a><span data-key="4c649e06e6b74f279b1df6b04fea0160"><span data-offset-key="4c649e06e6b74f279b1df6b04fea0160:0">.</span></span>

<span data-key="a5cfba5b360740c18011235be3b3698e"><span data-offset-key="a5cfba5b360740c18011235be3b3698e:0">Every deploy also has a permalink that starts with the deploy ID number. For example: </span>`1234abcd12acde000111cdef--yoursitename.netlify.app`<span data-offset-key="a5cfba5b360740c18011235be3b3698e:2">. The contents of this URL never change, even after you redeploy your site.</span></span>

<span data-key="5c99ac024bc44bd0bafc1a21e2cfb10a"><span data-offset-key="5c99ac024bc44bd0bafc1a21e2cfb10a:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://docs.netlify.com/site-deploys/deploy-previews/#collaborative-deploy-previews" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="40b22418547346cca62c4b6ae04f1b32" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="1033988b3a694a73b755e45b4f8e9379"><span data-offset-key="1033988b3a694a73b755e45b4f8e9379:0">#</span></span></span></a><span data-key="dfeebb5bdbf84cd09b6a62048cff40ca"><span data-offset-key="dfeebb5bdbf84cd09b6a62048cff40ca:0">Collaborative Deploy Previews</span></span>

<span data-key="1425ceb50d9041e48c24d3d71661b662"><span data-offset-key="1425ceb50d9041e48c24d3d71661b662:0">With collaborative Deploy Previews, you and your team can add, review, and manage feedback about site changes right from your site. You can leave comments, take screenshots and video, and test responsiveness on a mobile device.</span></span>

<span data-key="494ae8389a1c4231b14c275cfa204098"><span data-offset-key="494ae8389a1c4231b14c275cfa204098:0">You can access collaboration tools in the Netlify Drawer using the Netlify icon in your Deploy Preview.</span></span>

<span data-key="36d5c2a7eed243db889a5bfa4f0f7884"><span data-offset-key="36d5c2a7eed243db889a5bfa4f0f7884:0">Netlify Drawer icon</span></span>

### 

<span data-key="bfbc2da69ac74765a0fe70fd40e8dbf9"><span data-offset-key="bfbc2da69ac74765a0fe70fd40e8dbf9:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://docs.netlify.com/site-deploys/deploy-previews/#requirements-and-limitations" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="9ede14d8fb674813a6d988c6c2b5fc7b" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="9e3132ba57a348f088d927364b8db2da"><span data-offset-key="9e3132ba57a348f088d927364b8db2da:0">#</span></span></span></a><span data-key="0749b6c0cf3347199439ec90d8b01906"><span data-offset-key="0749b6c0cf3347199439ec90d8b01906:0">Requirements and limitations</span></span>

<span data-key="a3e24a5524164619b616e70ab233f405"><span data-offset-key="a3e24a5524164619b616e70ab233f405:0">Keep the following considerations in mind when working with collaborative Deploy Previews.</span></span>

<span data-key="0aaf3e370c234e9eb627665be8d9a958">**\#Requirements**</span>

-
