    <span data-key="ab325cbf4bfb4255890c35b6f4886f91">**Deploy Preview URLs**<span data-offset-key="ab325cbf4bfb4255890c35b6f4886f91:1">. Collaboration tools are only available on Deploy Previews accessed through their </span>`deploy-preview`<span data-offset-key="ab325cbf4bfb4255890c35b6f4886f91:3"> prefixed URLs.</span></span>

-   

    <span data-key="96eb074a883c46e089da4795c34f8dc7">**GitHub app permissions**<span data-offset-key="96eb074a883c46e089da4795c34f8dc7:1">. If you’re using GitHub, verify that the Netlify GitHub app is </span></span><a href="https://docs.netlify.com/configure-builds/repo-permissions-linking/#authentication-with-the-netlify-github-app" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="fb6f401b968a42c98ccf1e42dba1a40f" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="59f8b0b3e74048cfbf09f2d867dee06a"><span data-offset-key="59f8b0b3e74048cfbf09f2d867dee06a:0">installed with the necessary permissions</span></span></span></a><span data-key="6679040bdef24d679cd156698300b580"><span data-offset-key="6679040bdef24d679cd156698300b580:0">.</span></span>

-   

    <span data-key="8e47653ccd6b43f49fe5e14657b18a64">**Valid HTML**<span data-offset-key="8e47653ccd6b43f49fe5e14657b18a64:1">. Your site must have valid HTML output with opening and closing </span>`body`<span data-offset-key="8e47653ccd6b43f49fe5e14657b18a64:3"> tags.</span></span>

-   

    <span data-key="1079736ba6974415aa66809bf129c116">**Team access**<span data-offset-key="1079736ba6974415aa66809bf129c116:1">. Stakeholders must be signed into Netlify and </span></span><a href="https://docs.netlify.com/accounts-and-billing/team-management/manage-team-members" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="e488cb75a79a410d808b236af61f2493" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="9fee321f196747a19409305614827210"><span data-offset-key="9fee321f196747a19409305614827210:0">granted access</span></span></span></a><span data-key="773fbfaa91a04d81b2990d59c97fe52c"><span data-offset-key="773fbfaa91a04d81b2990d59c97fe52c:0"> to a team to use the collaboration tools. To request access to collaborate, select the </span>**Team Members**<span data-offset-key="773fbfaa91a04d81b2990d59c97fe52c:2"> tab and select </span>**Request to join team**<span data-offset-key="773fbfaa91a04d81b2990d59c97fe52c:4">.</span></span>

<span data-key="338e0c73d9634d90bf23a044f5f02f18">**\#Limitations**</span>

-   

    <span data-key="6504205965d94bbabc0df8d73f11d557">**On-demand Builders and server-side rendering**<span data-offset-key="6504205965d94bbabc0df8d73f11d557:1">. Collaboration tools are not available on sites using On-demand Builders or server-side rendering.</span></span>

-   

    <span data-key="7e10068a6f1f477295f2306d94760975">**Bitbucket**<span data-offset-key="7e10068a6f1f477295f2306d94760975:1">. Collaboration tools are currently not available on Bitbucket deploys.</span></span>

### 

<span data-key="c063b916aa4b43e3909d26e0c29c294e"><span data-offset-key="c063b916aa4b43e3909d26e0c29c294e:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://docs.netlify.com/site-deploys/deploy-previews/#give-feedback" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="78cdb0ac68ae4d2bb6b2e2964ae7d71b" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="edb3aa57506e430194e8685f5e81a60f"><span data-offset-key="edb3aa57506e430194e8685f5e81a60f:0">#</span></span></span></a><span data-key="2c3e5d0e17934aa5aa7aaea7f98d7077"><span data-offset-key="2c3e5d0e17934aa5aa7aaea7f98d7077:0">Give feedback</span></span>

<span data-key="891c5a5f953445e98ff6605100f21d8c"><span data-offset-key="891c5a5f953445e98ff6605100f21d8c:0">The Netlify Drawer provides access to a number of collaboration tools that team members and approved Reviewers can use to leave feedback about a Deploy Preview.</span></span>

<span data-key="9d95b8fd5faa49699d66647e5a0ce62b">**\#Leave comments**</span>

<span data-key="876e714c5d97471eb5f0cc9dc44f3a17"><span data-offset-key="876e714c5d97471eb5f0cc9dc44f3a17:0">Team members and approved Reviewers can leave comments on the Deploy Preview that are synced and mirrored on the GitHub pull request or GitLab merge request. Select the </span>**Activity**<span data-offset-key="876e714c5d97471eb5f0cc9dc44f3a17:2"> tab in the Netlify Drawer to start writing a comment.</span></span>

<span data-key="a3197310cf4f4e449d5443df4a6593df"><span data-offset-key="a3197310cf4f4e449d5443df4a6593df:0">If you are a pending Reviewer, your submitted comments will remain hidden until a team Owner or Collaborator approves you.</span></span>

<span data-key="c516839f9a1847c8b6d0dee53c5dd557">**\#Send feedback to third-party services**</span>

<span data-key="0ea29899fdc644a1bde01b8de7cf0f07"><span data-offset-key="0ea29899fdc644a1bde01b8de7cf0f07:0">You can send feedback about a Deploy Preview to a number of productivity tools by connecting your Netlify user account to your user account for the tool:</span></span>

-   

    <span data-key="74817ac36bcc4ae3921c507fb5318129"><span data-offset-key="74817ac36bcc4ae3921c507fb5318129:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://github.com/" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="f085dcfec1204356b3e35076d7eb5666" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="ec82723dab6d471cacd7b9954776f536"><span data-offset-key="ec82723dab6d471cacd7b9954776f536:0">GitHub</span></span></span></a><span data-key="a64ca38c200d4225baf0ea8293a2d985"><span data-offset-key="a64ca38c200d4225baf0ea8293a2d985:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>

-   

    <span data-key="de1efc3473594f5284f995f00b994d8b"><span data-offset-key="de1efc3473594f5284f995f00b994d8b:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://gitlab.com/" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="5b984e20742e4bbab6dd20c1fa5defbe" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="c06f0e2599e042d89bb10b21c730d32c"><span data-offset-key="c06f0e2599e042d89bb10b21c730d32c:0">GitLab</span></span></span></a><span data-key="ca735d9134fb44208b4adcc00ca53c3e"><span data-offset-key="ca735d9134fb44208b4adcc00ca53c3e:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>

-   

    <span data-key="c6773f1122b448f4bf779f2357562ff5"><span data-offset-key="c6773f1122b448f4bf779f2357562ff5:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://www.atlassian.com/software/jira" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="79ff8bbc75b7463b95560595b5b91144" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="d10e54b2f642409ba94035bbab9f2e3e"><span data-offset-key="d10e54b2f642409ba94035bbab9f2e3e:0">Jira Software</span></span></span></a><span data-key="f5ade76743f14e4b98f560ae7dccc96b"><span data-offset-key="f5ade76743f14e4b98f560ae7dccc96b:0"> (may not be available on all </span></span><a href="https://www.netlify.com/pricing/" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="2e4de4d6240b4793a4eab4a4c28affa4" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="a797be9437af4b6ca8dcb5e891dd6fd3"><span data-offset-key="a797be9437af4b6ca8dcb5e891dd6fd3:0">plans</span></span></span></a><span data-key="ac89779b3db94fd7a78d6cb8bd13d69c"><span data-offset-key="ac89779b3db94fd7a78d6cb8bd13d69c:0">)</span></span>

-   

    <span data-key="3be0fd272a9247f083b20bc5d20f38b8"><span data-offset-key="3be0fd272a9247f083b20bc5d20f38b8:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://shortcut.com/" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="8f0af963844947e4b36be7a25a344fd2" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="9adfba77624944f082d56c6a1fdd8d00"><span data-offset-key="9adfba77624944f082d56c6a1fdd8d00:0">Shortcut</span></span></span></a><span data-key="02a22b8ce4e9411db3f966fdba15df1c"><span data-offset-key="02a22b8ce4e9411db3f966fdba15df1c:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>

-   

    <span data-key="8aca1750d66f4bfa8db5f7f584793597"><span data-offset-key="8aca1750d66f4bfa8db5f7f584793597:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://linear.app/" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="1b031c5e135e4b078d3d585729b785e2" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="4b67a97958c74d1fa887e20cfeb83b8e"><span data-offset-key="4b67a97958c74d1fa887e20cfeb83b8e:0">Linear</span></span></span></a><span data-key="9b76f3cd23884e38bc2c225e509163e3"><span data-offset-key="9b76f3cd23884e38bc2c225e509163e3:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>

-   

    <span data-key="1c69e4b858004093b263f824219dc6c3"><span data-offset-key="1c69e4b858004093b263f824219dc6c3:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://trello.com/" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="2b1fa826fe9c46ebb193c6f02e2a9487" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="0684368b9a674a8eb3f7974cde5a0fff"><span data-offset-key="0684368b9a674a8eb3f7974cde5a0fff:0">Trello</span></span></span></a><span data-key="0c3cf1ee965a4c699d58ca31e2c8323b"><span data-offset-key="0c3cf1ee965a4c699d58ca31e2c8323b:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>

<span data-key="fdf505376f814051afd9a8d578ce49bd"><span data-offset-key="fdf505376f814051afd9a8d578ce49bd:0">To get started, go to the </span>**Integrations**<span data-offset-key="fdf505376f814051afd9a8d578ce49bd:2"> tab in the Netlify Drawer and select </span>**Connect**<span data-offset-key="fdf505376f814051afd9a8d578ce49bd:4"> for the third-party service you want to use.</span></span>

<span data-key="c888642646be4ddfb4cc2734f2b9108e"><span data-offset-key="c888642646be4ddfb4cc2734f2b9108e:0">Netlify Drawer Integrations tab</span></span>

<span data-key="6b106f624f8948e697388bf4c0c57276"><span data-offset-key="6b106f624f8948e697388bf4c0c57276:0">Once your Netlify user account is connected to a third-party service, you can submit feedback to the service directly from the Deploy Preview by selecting </span>**New issue**<span data-offset-key="6b106f624f8948e697388bf4c0c57276:2">.</span></span>

<span data-key="b8dc9d4b72994741bee953698a149cba">**\#Take screenshots and record screen**</span>

<span data-key="6332453b5b2f49abb4eee95524842f4c"><span data-offset-key="6332453b5b2f49abb4eee95524842f4c:0">You can take a screenshot or screen recording and use it in feedback in the pull/merge request or third-party integration.</span></span>

<span data-key="b016f7e8799d4bbab1e2a4a8da304985"><span data-offset-key="b016f7e8799d4bbab1e2a4a8da304985:0">To add a screenshot, hover over the Netlify icon and select </span>**Take screenshot**<span data-offset-key="b016f7e8799d4bbab1e2a4a8da304985:2">. You can edit and annotate your screenshot before using it in feedback.</span></span>

<span data-key="e657ce8b2c414d6dbc560c8929ce4816"><span data-offset-key="e657ce8b2c414d6dbc560c8929ce4816:0">To record a screen interaction, hover over the Netlify icon and select </span>**Record screen**<span data-offset-key="e657ce8b2c414d6dbc560c8929ce4816:2">. You can use the screen recording in your feedback as a GIF.</span></span>

<span data-key="49e980953e644d74b9068599574f575b"><span data-offset-key="49e980953e644d74b9068599574f575b:0">You can also drag and drop image and video files directly onto the </span>**Activity tab**<span data-offset-key="49e980953e644d74b9068599574f575b:2"> text area to include them in a comment using Markdown syntax.</span></span>

### 

<span data-key="79f4b487e2844b02afa1ab0d3470f65b"><span data-offset-key="79f4b487e2844b02afa1ab0d3470f65b:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://docs.netlify.com/site-deploys/deploy-previews/#get-feedback" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="7f746050836249e8bb74e6ac8dc0ab30" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="6fac5359fc30433b8520a044520c5dbc"><span data-offset-key="6fac5359fc30433b8520a044520c5dbc:0">#</span></span></span></a><span data-key="1b84c853f1e14996834530c876f5f409"><span data-offset-key="1b84c853f1e14996834530c876f5f409:0">Get feedback</span></span>

<span data-key="3c6e194507f9472f82ca083c25b9bd70"><span data-offset-key="3c6e194507f9472f82ca083c25b9bd70:0">The Netlify Drawer also provides tools for team Owners and Collaborators to request feedback about a Deploy Preview.</span></span>

<span data-key="af6241414d6240f0845e17f560ee4982">**\#Invite contributors**</span>

<span data-key="da115eee77d24db39ac9ed6df3c87bfc"><span data-offset-key="da115eee77d24db39ac9ed6df3c87bfc:0">You can select </span>**Add members**<span data-offset-key="da115eee77d24db39ac9ed6df3c87bfc:2"> to invite users to join your team, including an unlimited number of free Reviewers.</span></span>

<span data-key="3d4831289aad48adbae5cfd51fd22076"><span data-offset-key="3d4831289aad48adbae5cfd51fd22076:0">For more information on team member permissions, check the </span></span><a href="https://docs.netlify.com/accounts-and-billing/team-management/manage-team-members/#team-roles" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="b4945e909929404fa2ee0952ab6804a1" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="89ad2df27bfb4241bb51cb45f06e533a"><span data-offset-key="89ad2df27bfb4241bb51cb45f06e533a:0">team roles</span></span></span></a><span data-key="784f8449136b473db951169cd5483dcf"><span data-offset-key="784f8449136b473db951169cd5483dcf:0"> documentation.</span></span>

<span data-key="4a9fbdfbfa0a4aed8482edfdade5c03f">**\#Set entry path**</span>

<span data-key="6f66d3214fc94f93be2da96a588d03f8"><span data-offset-key="6f66d3214fc94f93be2da96a588d03f8:0">The entry path is the page visitors will land on when they access your Deploy Preview using links on the </span>**Deploys**<span data-offset-key="6f66d3214fc94f93be2da96a588d03f8:2"> page, deploy details page, in GitHub, or in GitLab. You can set an entry path in the following ways:</span></span>

-   

    <span data-key="2a040c1c5f4e43c8a4835f6af33083ce"><span data-offset-key="2a040c1c5f4e43c8a4835f6af33083ce:0">Enter the path in the </span>**Settings**<span data-offset-key="2a040c1c5f4e43c8a4835f6af33083ce:2"> tab of the Netlify Drawer.</span></span>

-   

    <span data-key="3a283960b007450a965efd477b0e8b28"><span data-offset-key="3a283960b007450a965efd477b0e8b28:0">Tag </span>`@netlify /path/to/page`<span data-offset-key="3a283960b007450a965efd477b0e8b28:2"> in the initial description of your GitHub pull request or GitLab merge request.</span></span>

-   

    <span data-key="cbadbf06ebbe4c129be45ed7b9cdfdbc"><span data-offset-key="cbadbf06ebbe4c129be45ed7b9cdfdbc:0">Hover over the Netlify icon and select </span>**Set as entry path**<span data-offset-key="cbadbf06ebbe4c129be45ed7b9cdfdbc:2"> to save the current page as the initial route. This option only appears if you are the author of the pull/merge request.</span></span>

<span data-key="20f4428b2d464f7a9251d8c2e3c147a1"><span data-offset-key="20f4428b2d464f7a9251d8c2e3c147a1:0">When writing a value for the entry path, it must be relative and start with </span>`/`<span data-offset-key="20f4428b2d464f7a9251d8c2e3c147a1:2">.</span></span>

### 

<span data-key="5d71977d78d944ba8dc10b7b554f2ed1"><span data-offset-key="5d71977d78d944ba8dc10b7b554f2ed1:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://docs.netlify.com/site-deploys/deploy-previews/#test-and-troubleshoot-with-collaboration-tools" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="63fa9e2202ae452597a6787f82c39245" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="2aecbc0bc1c44b88be69d301ab25a69f"><span data-offset-key="2aecbc0bc1c44b88be69d301ab25a69f:0">#</span></span></span></a><span data-key="59f81ddc3d3c485a9c0edaa57adf8938"><span data-offset-key="59f81ddc3d3c485a9c0edaa57adf8938:0">Test and troubleshoot with collaboration tools</span></span>

<span data-key="aef21adf94d9401d98a1eebdd52a0a38"><span data-offset-key="aef21adf94d9401d98a1eebdd52a0a38:0">The Netlify Drawer provides access to tools that team Owners, Collaborators, and Reviewers can use to test and troubleshoot specific site deploys.</span></span>

<span data-key="cdd185f182854085b52a44f162537e67">**\#Monitor logs**</span>

<span data-key="a958c17c66cb4be5b6da9ac66217bf6f"><span data-offset-key="a958c17c66cb4be5b6da9ac66217bf6f:0">Owners and Collaborators can access the deploy log and serverless function logs in the Netlify Drawer to help with monitoring and troubleshooting a specific deploy.</span></span>

<span data-key="a3b9eb65f60a4ec0ae42099513b1ff95"><span data-offset-key="a3b9eb65f60a4ec0ae42099513b1ff95:0">To find details about the deploy, open the </span>**Deploy Logs**<span data-offset-key="a3b9eb65f60a4ec0ae42099513b1ff95:2"> tab of the Netlify Drawer. Visit our </span></span><a href="https://docs.netlify.com/site-deploys/overview/#deploy-log" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="c75a635b00e64ec185274be49107a18d" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="a54f264b24c145b3b0564f12bd8f2c5f"><span data-offset-key="a54f264b24c145b3b0564f12bd8f2c5f:0">deploy log docs</span></span></span></a><span data-key="b3e50829454e436eb95d738473165c49"><span data-offset-key="b3e50829454e436eb95d738473165c49:0"> for more information.</span></span>

<span data-key="da4835e683534693bef95e1d608ddf5f"><span data-offset-key="da4835e683534693bef95e1d608ddf5f:0">You can access serverless function logs by opening the </span>**Function logs**<span data-offset-key="da4835e683534693bef95e1d608ddf5f:2"> tab in the Netlify Drawer and selecting a function to check out its latest log contents for the current session. Visit our </span></span><a href="https://docs.netlify.com/functions/logs/" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="1c2ac411ccec428296e5145ecb570d57" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="25ce06918ab8449b8c8bf273cc222ba0"><span data-offset-key="25ce06918ab8449b8c8bf273cc222ba0:0">Function logs docs</span></span></span></a><span data-key="750fdc1ef94f41fbad94572324804a1e"><span data-offset-key="750fdc1ef94f41fbad94572324804a1e:0"> for more information.</span></span>

<span data-key="6d6e69ff916342d1bdd2ddc21eecc72d">**\#Check responsiveness and site performance**</span>

<span data-key="d64f89bb127d417a83b5e3394ed23821"><span data-offset-key="d64f89bb127d417a83b5e3394ed23821:0">You can open your Deploy Preview on your mobile device to check your site’s performance and test responsiveness. To open your Deploy Preview on a mobile device, hover over the Netlify icon and select </span>**Open on device**<span data-offset-key="d64f89bb127d417a83b5e3394ed23821:2">. You can then scan the QR code with your device to open the page.</span></span>

<span data-key="1c2e185d8b6748f7b4888edd30eb432d">**\#Access browser details and replicate in BrowserStack**</span>

<span data-key="3f544cd70bb44c75851edd4208450bb7"><span data-offset-key="3f544cd70bb44c75851edd4208450bb7:0">When someone shares feedback through a collaborative Deploy Preview, you can access metadata about the browser the comment author used. You can also replicate their browser environment for testing and QA through a built-in integration with </span></span><a href="https://www.browserstack.com/" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="c2d680015e9e4857be9565789c181f90" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="9d3d64b0cf974ec98294ef68d462110e"><span data-offset-key="9d3d64b0cf974ec98294ef68d462110e:0">BrowserStack</span></span></span></a><span data-key="807cc986d703412090751e3a7b2171e9"><span data-offset-key="807cc986d703412090751e3a7b2171e9:0">.</span></span>

<span data-key="95e5f1fe86bc43d1ae3c1e720b18e1e4"><span data-offset-key="95e5f1fe86bc43d1ae3c1e720b18e1e4:0">In collaborative Deploy Preview feedback, find the browser information (usually near the bottom of the feedback) and select </span>**Open in BrowserStack**<span data-offset-key="95e5f1fe86bc43d1ae3c1e720b18e1e4:2"> to launch a BrowserStack instance that matches the author of the comment’s browser, browser version, viewport size, and operating system.</span></span>

<span data-key="6d83966fae994dfebcece9c6a18cf260"><span data-offset-key="6d83966fae994dfebcece9c6a18cf260:0">The BrowserStack service provides a free </span></span><a href="https://www.netlify.com/blog/2021/07/20/troubleshoot-qa-issues-faster-with-browserstack-and-deploy-previews/#extended-free-browserstack-minutes-for-netlify-users" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="3cc91eb32d724ca28456a757ab0911da" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="a916710a6e2a427b8893338951ca5588"><span data-offset-key="a916710a6e2a427b8893338951ca5588:0">60 minute total usage allotment</span></span></span></a><span data-key="bb2d9bb40e2441ab963b7095e32941b0"><span data-offset-key="bb2d9bb40e2441ab963b7095e32941b0:0"> for users who sign up from Netlify. An option to upgrade is available in BrowserStack once the allotment is finished.</span></span>

### 

<span data-key="7d1551b8591248c29fb9a4a57f517c0a"><span data-offset-key="7d1551b8591248c29fb9a4a57f517c0a:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://docs.netlify.com/site-deploys/deploy-previews/#troubleshooting-collaborative-deploy-previews" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="7ec09386af0b4d4ba8f5733b8837e176" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="01ec9c4696dc4e8f8e25f159704b97b8"><span data-offset-key="01ec9c4696dc4e8f8e25f159704b97b8:0">#</span></span></span></a><span data-key="457f0a19fd9a4bd4bb0dad2fc8e8333f"><span data-offset-key="457f0a19fd9a4bd4bb0dad2fc8e8333f:0">Troubleshooting collaborative Deploy Previews</span></span>

<span data-key="9f85519d271447a5aee21b0ece5ba080"><span data-offset-key="9f85519d271447a5aee21b0ece5ba080:0">This section provides troubleshooting tips for using and accessing collaborative Deploy Previews. Make sure you have reviewed the </span></span><a href="https://docs.netlify.com/site-deploys/deploy-previews/#requirements" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="25bce21f32f54ddcb293c790be751412" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="c0456b48c5e04f89b1206ba87389e167"><span data-offset-key="c0456b48c5e04f89b1206ba87389e167:0">requirements</span></span></span></a><span data-key="f4b49fa66c8641de9d687f34aa3303b3"><span data-offset-key="f4b49fa66c8641de9d687f34aa3303b3:0"> and </span></span><a href="https://docs.netlify.com/site-deploys/deploy-previews/#limitations" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="b7e5214c7d88493f9c875433abb2faa4" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="b850bd8cc987462eb69b48baac22711e"><span data-offset-key="b850bd8cc987462eb69b48baac22711e:0">limitations</span></span></span></a><span data-key="59b72c0452ef4415b58772075dca2db9"><span data-offset-key="59b72c0452ef4415b58772075dca2db9:0"> for collaborative Deploy Previews before you begin.</span></span>

<span data-key="105f2ca02fa44c1cb2925abdf0c4185a"><span data-offset-key="105f2ca02fa44c1cb2925abdf0c4185a:0">If you have additional concerns that aren’t answered here, you can visit our </span></span><a href="https://answers.netlify.com/categories" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="5c87214c28034dea834f31c6cab7f19c" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="160f8414a71e4da58c10c62e4d3a69cf"><span data-offset-key="160f8414a71e4da58c10c62e4d3a69cf:0">Forums</span></span></span></a><span data-key="c4717547df9b493e9cabd5446f13b9cf"><span data-offset-key="c4717547df9b493e9cabd5446f13b9cf:0"> to ask questions and find more information.</span></span>

<span data-key="e1d4802111f349759cad8a6ee88b2f28">**\#Netlify Drawer is missing**</span>

<span data-key="1915feed410642eeb50912a23651cf5a"><span data-offset-key="1915feed410642eeb50912a23651cf5a:0">If you can’t find the Netlify Drawer on your Deploy Preview, verify that the Netlify Drawer is enabled for your site. You can do this by going to your site in the Netlify UI and selecting </span>**Site settings &gt; Build & deploy &gt; Continuous Deployment &gt; Deploy Previews**<span data-offset-key="1915feed410642eeb50912a23651cf5a:2">.</span></span>

<span data-key="a070652b29a94f8da3f95c2b3fdf0130"><span data-offset-key="a070652b29a94f8da3f95c2b3fdf0130:0">The Netlify Drawer also might not appear if your site’s </span></span><a href="https://docs.netlify.com/routing/headers/" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="62d434a4057941d093bc9ec01b30d04e" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="e6d7746fa1ed43bdb65c8dbddc806a1f"><span data-offset-key="e6d7746fa1ed43bdb65c8dbddc806a1f:0">custom headers</span></span></span></a><span data-key="a5ea9712c1644048a082d7f7de6c59b0"><span data-offset-key="a5ea9712c1644048a082d7f7de6c59b0:0"> include the following Content Security Policy (CSP) directives:</span></span>

-   

    <span data-key="d824e3b05d2e4976bd95b7c1baccb8c2">`default-src`</span>

-   

    <span data-key="fad2049170e341289d90450a9a94d8ac">`script-src`</span>

-   

    <span data-key="df995577ac4c494297ac783434b361c1">`frame-src`</span>

-   

    <span data-key="85dec20e8c1f4ea1bc3462ab1587df7c">`child-src`</span>

<span data-key="6eb38db942d34b578e2bd70a6ff4e3fb"><span data-offset-key="6eb38db942d34b578e2bd70a6ff4e3fb:0">To address this issue, add </span>`app.netlify.com`<span data-offset-key="6eb38db942d34b578e2bd70a6ff4e3fb:2"> and </span>`netlify-cdp-loader.netlify.app`<span data-offset-key="6eb38db942d34b578e2bd70a6ff4e3fb:4"> to the allow list in the </span>`_headers`<span data-offset-key="6eb38db942d34b578e2bd70a6ff4e3fb:6"> or </span>`netlify.toml`<span data-offset-key="6eb38db942d34b578e2bd70a6ff4e3fb:8"> file. For example:</span></span>

-   

    <span data-key="85b8feed0f3e43bab576f9d94833fa7f"><span data-offset-key="85b8feed0f3e43bab576f9d94833fa7f:0">\_headers</span></span>

-   

    <span data-key="11d5ade085ba43bf8aa7d0509e4f666e"><span data-offset-key="11d5ade085ba43bf8aa7d0509e4f666e:0">netlify.toml</span></span>

1

<span data-key="dda47970405b4431ab1e676845242c16"><span data-offset-key="dda47970405b4431ab1e676845242c16:0">/\*</span></span>

2

<span data-key="05d9ffa62071403e96c7520a6985feaf"><span data-offset-key="05d9ffa62071403e96c7520a6985feaf:0"> Content-Security-Policy: child-src 'self' app.netlify.com; script-src 'self' app.netlify.com netlify-cdp-loader.netlify.app;</span></span>

Copied!

<span data-key="c958e91549bc48a48c5a6efd9c7d0c4f">**\#Netlify Drawer blocks content**</span>

<span data-key="5b048ad874b346859ef33573338725f0"><span data-offset-key="5b048ad874b346859ef33573338725f0:0">If the Netlify Drawer is blocking important UI elements, you can drag and drop the icon and pin it to any of the four corners of your screen.</span></span>

<span data-key="7fb5fdcb31ef4fbf8b7cfe02f9440ad2">**\#Reviewer comments appear as a different GitLab user**</span>

<span data-key="639e69acf83f412780d8906b270c4f36"><span data-offset-key="639e69acf83f412780d8906b270c4f36:0">If a Reviewer authenticates with GitLab, comments they add through collaboration tools in a Deploy Preview are mirrored in a merge request using their GitLab profile. If a Reviewer doesn’t authenticate with GitLab or doesn’t have a GitLab account, comments mirrored in a merge request appear under the profile of the GitLab user who configured the site on Netlify. These mirrored comments start with </span>**A reviewer left a comment**<span data-offset-key="639e69acf83f412780d8906b270c4f36:2">.</span></span>

<span data-key="ac714f0ad3bf48e9acb6eff0469d0872"><span data-offset-key="ac714f0ad3bf48e9acb6eff0469d0872:0">To change the GitLab user for unauthenticated comments on merge requests, a GitLab project Owner or Maintainer can take these steps:</span></span>

1.  <span class="r-1awozwy r-1nf4jbm r-6koalj r-18u37iz r-gg6oyi r-ubezar r-16dba41 r-135wba7 r-1m04atk r-1pyaxff" contenteditable="false" style="height: 24px">1.</span>
    <span data-key="1f16751425e14935853604b4fbc590ab"><span data-offset-key="1f16751425e14935853604b4fbc590ab:0">In GitLab, invite a new user with a role of Reporter or above to your project. The email address for this user must be one you have access to.</span></span>

2.  <span class="r-1awozwy r-1nf4jbm r-6koalj r-18u37iz r-gg6oyi r-ubezar r-16dba41 r-135wba7 r-1m04atk r-1pyaxff" contenteditable="false" style="height: 24px">2.</span>
    <span data-key="3fbdffa0a76c464f83ff4fe78302f46b"><span data-offset-key="3fbdffa0a76c464f83ff4fe78302f46b:0">Confirm the user and log into GitLab with that account.</span></span>

3.  <span class="r-1awozwy r-1nf4jbm r-6koalj r-18u37iz r-gg6oyi r-ubezar r-16dba41 r-135wba7 r-1m04atk r-1pyaxff" contenteditable="false" style="height: 24px">3.</span>
    <span data-key="6f8322f14d224fc8ae3b27f6770efc5e"><span data-offset-key="6f8322f14d224fc8ae3b27f6770efc5e:0">Edit the </span></span><a href="https://gitlab.com/-/profile" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="7adf2437a2be4ea78120502e47f6fae9" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="c8ff61ce4a3f43ac905c38a710651659"><span data-offset-key="c8ff61ce4a3f43ac905c38a710651659:0">GitLab profile</span></span></span></a><span data-key="9b19229bf0ba49fbb0872a108d1c7e21"><span data-offset-key="9b19229bf0ba49fbb0872a108d1c7e21:0"> of the user to change the </span>**Full name**<span data-offset-key="9b19229bf0ba49fbb0872a108d1c7e21:2"> and </span>**Public avatar**<span data-offset-key="9b19229bf0ba49fbb0872a108d1c7e21:4">. We recommend naming the user </span>`Netlify`<span data-offset-key="9b19229bf0ba49fbb0872a108d1c7e21:6"> and using the Netlify logo as the avatar to help associate unauthenticated comments with Netlify.</span></span>

4.  <span class="r-1awozwy r-1nf4jbm r-6koalj r-18u37iz r-gg6oyi r-ubezar r-16dba41 r-135wba7 r-1m04atk r-1pyaxff" contenteditable="false" style="height: 24px">4.</span>
    <span data-key="c4ce69781283447088c60d6f37223e0f"><span data-offset-key="c4ce69781283447088c60d6f37223e0f:0">Generate a </span></span><a href="https://gitlab.com/-/profile/personal_access_tokens" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="87787dc41f5a4d57bcab002fb4840247" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="9930da6df4a144c7b1bc02c317409215"><span data-offset-key="9930da6df4a144c7b1bc02c317409215:0">personal access token</span></span></span></a><span data-key="f1195ef1c4a54bf69fefeda49c562a07"><span data-offset-key="f1195ef1c4a54bf69fefeda49c562a07:0"> with an </span>`api`<span data-offset-key="f1195ef1c4a54bf69fefeda49c562a07:2"> scope, and copy the token to your clipboard.</span></span>

5.  <span class="r-1awozwy r-1nf4jbm r-6koalj r-18u37iz r-gg6oyi r-ubezar r-16dba41 r-135wba7 r-1m04atk r-1pyaxff" contenteditable="false" style="height: 24px">5.</span>
    <span data-key="b6df2c9547974e7babb3cb3c08035f5c"><span data-offset-key="b6df2c9547974e7babb3cb3c08035f5c:0">In a Deploy Preview from one of your GitLab sites, open the </span>**Deploy settings**<span data-offset-key="b6df2c9547974e7babb3cb3c08035f5c:2"> tab in the Netlify Drawer. Paste in the token from GitLab, and select </span>**Save**<span data-offset-key="b6df2c9547974e7babb3cb3c08035f5c:4">.</span></span>

    <span data-key="3f04885365bd4a8aa2f41dcd08a0a14f"><span data-offset-key="3f04885365bd4a8aa2f41dcd08a0a14f:0">Comments left by Reviewers who have not authenticated with GitLab should now be associated with the Netlify user on your project.</span></span>

<span data-key="3fc86a2df6204495afe053e6e4d73058">**\#Preview changes without the Netlify Drawer**</span>

<span data-key="6502a8fff8f549b9a40f1ed83949a775"><span data-offset-key="6502a8fff8f549b9a40f1ed83949a775:0">To opt out of loading the Netlify Drawer on a site’s Deploy Previews, go to </span>**Site settings &gt; Build & deploy &gt; Continuous Deployment &gt; Deploy Previews**<span data-offset-key="6502a8fff8f549b9a40f1ed83949a775:2">, select </span>**Edit settings**<span data-offset-key="6502a8fff8f549b9a40f1ed83949a775:4">, and disable the Netlify Drawer.</span></span>

<span data-key="e63e99ae95f44ce09f85c64268a569b4"><span data-offset-key="e63e99ae95f44ce09f85c64268a569b4:0">You can also open a </span></span><a href="https://docs.netlify.com/site-deploys/overview/#definitions" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="069747056ab44bc09798b35f360ca2f1" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="05699cd6fcf24d96a4c17537f5d38748"><span data-offset-key="05699cd6fcf24d96a4c17537f5d38748:0">branch deploy or deploy permalink</span></span></span></a><span data-key="939a824a29a046e9a8a28d6cbd44c5b5"><span data-offset-key="939a824a29a046e9a8a28d6cbd44c5b5:0"> if you need to preview a deploy but don’t want to access any of the collaboration features. Both links are available in the Netlify Drawer under </span>**Settings**<span data-offset-key="939a824a29a046e9a8a28d6cbd44c5b5:2">. The branch deploy link is also available on your site’s </span>**Deploys**<span data-offset-key="939a824a29a046e9a8a28d6cbd44c5b5:4"> page in the Netlify UI, while the deploy permalink is available on the deploy details page.</span></span>

<span data-key="cec7e6d72f474405b6cf262460e52127"><span data-offset-key="cec7e6d72f474405b6cf262460e52127:0">Post processing</span></span>

<span data-key="2813e9a2ab0a4e349562f5192f590b05"><span data-offset-key="2813e9a2ab0a4e349562f5192f590b05:0">Netlify offers several post processing features to help you optimize your sites. These are available under </span>**Site settings &gt; Build & deploy &gt; Post processing**<span data-offset-key="2813e9a2ab0a4e349562f5192f590b05:2">.</span></span>

<span data-key="ad2a035a2404426c9072d88f538f8a80"><span data-offset-key="ad2a035a2404426c9072d88f538f8a80:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://docs.netlify.com/site-deploys/post-processing/#post-processing-features" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="80af67cc93f1404eb0ce5d4f280da663" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="9c5456b899904835a9470363420d1ee0"><span data-offset-key="9c5456b899904835a9470363420d1ee0:0">#</span></span></span></a><span data-key="e53525ad17f4447586935ec1fa6ac4c4"><span data-offset-key="e53525ad17f4447586935ec1fa6ac4c4:0">Post processing features</span></span>

<span data-key="6e7fef36d8064f548ffe3bd40e5d47c3">**Snippet injection**<span data-offset-key="6e7fef36d8064f548ffe3bd40e5d47c3:1"> - Analytics or other scripts can be added to the HTML of your site using </span></span><a href="https://docs.netlify.com/site-deploys/post-processing/snippet-injection/" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="0d7ea53c82a74d899da2ba0051740967" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="a8fea68ace9a4d8a8602eecfcf78da31"><span data-offset-key="a8fea68ace9a4d8a8602eecfcf78da31:0">snippet injection</span></span></span></a><span data-key="eac0d635fa414eae8e50af32ef1ff357"><span data-offset-key="eac0d635fa414eae8e50af32ef1ff357:0">.</span></span>

<span data-key="ab03757bfa094cb99887d261509ae90b">**Asset optimization**<span data-offset-key="ab03757bfa094cb99887d261509ae90b:1"> - You can rewrite link URLs to pretty URLs, bundle and minify CSS and JS, and compress images. These options can be controlled via </span></span><a href="https://docs.netlify.com/configure-builds/file-based-configuration/#post-processing" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="4fe0dd6322d947c796252a14797446d0" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="2db8d6ab49a7424c920e9806b4fd9e0a"><span data-offset-key="2db8d6ab49a7424c920e9806b4fd9e0a:0">file-based configuration</span></span></span></a><span data-key="259c36c2d77c4f8eac24dc58bb8c87e5"><span data-offset-key="259c36c2d77c4f8eac24dc58bb8c87e5:0"> as well as in </span>**Site settings**<span data-offset-key="259c36c2d77c4f8eac24dc58bb8c87e5:2">.</span></span>

<span data-key="46871e90c46e4797a6b522b4994f831b">**Prerendering**<span data-offset-key="46871e90c46e4797a6b522b4994f831b:1"> - To allow search engines and social networks to crawl the pages rendered by your app, you can enable </span></span><a href="https://docs.netlify.com/site-deploys/post-processing/prerendering/" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="04b41eed47ea42d5a2edf4b6f5470d38" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="2b8436258ee448db94f9a72cea638aec"><span data-offset-key="2b8436258ee448db94f9a72cea638aec:0">prerendering</span></span></span></a><span data-key="f407eb9ae1134ea59d6806ee3aa5dffe"><span data-offset-key="f407eb9ae1134ea59d6806ee3aa5dffe:0">.</span></span>

<span data-key="997b4ecf4d3041d7af4b194d3eb94332">**Form detection**<span data-offset-key="997b4ecf4d3041d7af4b194d3eb94332:1"> - By default, Netlify scans new and updated HTML files to detect forms and set them up for receiving submissions. You can disable </span></span><a href="https://docs.netlify.com/site-deploys/post-processing/form-detection/" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="c053171120294f06a292377ab215f64c" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="8f11fe452f8546adb4dfa487cd604170"><span data-offset-key="8f11fe452f8546adb4dfa487cd604170:0">form detection</span></span></span></a><span data-key="88e644ef286f458987f00fd20d017a20"><span data-offset-key="88e644ef286f458987f00fd20d017a20:0"> to speed up deploys if you’re not using Forms.</span></span>

<span data-key="1c2cc217e40e4a73b810f78c19e4d8d1"><span data-offset-key="1c2cc217e40e4a73b810f78c19e4d8d1:0">Snippet injection</span></span>

<span data-key="e3efee933cf6482db94fc84034730c47"><span data-offset-key="e3efee933cf6482db94fc84034730c47:0">Often you want to inject JavaScript snippets into all pages of your site, either in the </span>`<head>`<span data-offset-key="e3efee933cf6482db94fc84034730c47:2"> or at the end of the </span>`<body>`<span data-offset-key="e3efee933cf6482db94fc84034730c47:4"> tag.</span></span>

<span data-key="a49bd23833294e5dbd05bdf54995a2b0"><span data-offset-key="a49bd23833294e5dbd05bdf54995a2b0:0">Most analytics providers, retargeting services, and A/B testing services will give you an HTML snippet and ask you to add it to every page on your site. Netlify lets you do this without having to pollute the source code for the site with production specific analytics snippets.</span></span>

<span data-key="931463c12f3b41759f1b7a6e6742c9d9"><span data-offset-key="931463c12f3b41759f1b7a6e6742c9d9:0">You can pick between injecting the scripts before the closing </span>`</head>`<span data-offset-key="931463c12f3b41759f1b7a6e6742c9d9:2"> tag or before the closing </span>`</body>`<span data-offset-key="931463c12f3b41759f1b7a6e6742c9d9:4"> tag.</span></span>

<span data-key="5b0116962ebe4b06ab6933e5f7025042"><span data-offset-key="5b0116962ebe4b06ab6933e5f7025042:0">Note</span></span>

<span data-key="a7455360faeb47cba9ff8c38fc71a1fa"><span data-offset-key="a7455360faeb47cba9ff8c38fc71a1fa:0">Injected snippets will also show up on the </span>`password`<span data-offset-key="a7455360faeb47cba9ff8c38fc71a1fa:2"> protection screen. This means you can verify that your analytics scripts are correctly configured without having to remove the password when your site is still under development.</span></span>

<span data-key="3591eaa6674b4d9e8625225aed21da26"><span data-offset-key="3591eaa6674b4d9e8625225aed21da26:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://docs.netlify.com/site-deploys/post-processing/snippet-injection/#snippet-injection-ui" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="965fc615fb174ddbacd60c60c0ff67f5" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="863b3f153586439ab6a51c3a151204ae"><span data-offset-key="863b3f153586439ab6a51c3a151204ae:0">#</span></span></span></a><span data-key="d08aa07ca48441609868b5eb9017c5b3"><span data-offset-key="d08aa07ca48441609868b5eb9017c5b3:0">Snippet injection UI</span></span>

<span data-key="dc272c5448714240bb05fdea283f325b"><span data-offset-key="dc272c5448714240bb05fdea283f325b:0">In </span>**Site settings &gt; Build & Deploy &gt; Post processing**<span data-offset-key="dc272c5448714240bb05fdea283f325b:2">, find the </span>**Snippet Injection**<span data-offset-key="dc272c5448714240bb05fdea283f325b:4"> section and select </span>**Add Snippet**<span data-offset-key="dc272c5448714240bb05fdea283f325b:6">. Then give your script a name and paste the script body (including any </span>`<script>`<span data-offset-key="dc272c5448714240bb05fdea283f325b:8"> tags, etc).</span></span>

<span data-key="13ff517eebb141f8bf949ffe634757b7"><span data-offset-key="13ff517eebb141f8bf949ffe634757b7:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://docs.netlify.com/site-deploys/post-processing/snippet-injection/#api-endpoints" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="e9164fbdc8b84413b7f5e3856fdba72c" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="0b17137870bd4ad6a727912e3302ce6f"><span data-offset-key="0b17137870bd4ad6a727912e3302ce6f:0">#</span></span></span></a><span data-key="dd4266af71014468b80f3791143fbb8d"><span data-offset-key="dd4266af71014468b80f3791143fbb8d:0">API endpoints</span></span>

<span data-key="e4505106b976492d8e03e611faf38839"><span data-offset-key="e4505106b976492d8e03e611faf38839:0">You can use the </span></span><a href="https://docs.netlify.com/api/get-started/#snippets" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="933adace0c0b403e8f0ee835ea6a9f8f" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="d84249743fbe40ae89c6fa26439a16c9"><span data-offset-key="d84249743fbe40ae89c6fa26439a16c9:0">API</span></span></span></a><span data-key="ebf422366a4145919d852061cc687804"><span data-offset-key="ebf422366a4145919d852061cc687804:0"> to get snippets, add snippets, and more.</span></span>

<span data-key="dbf160ff985f473e974fa80dae05a6ad"><span data-offset-key="dbf160ff985f473e974fa80dae05a6ad:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://docs.netlify.com/site-deploys/post-processing/snippet-injection/#more-resources" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="38fbb1fd9b1b498483f0d8c1a6935ba3" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="4b9b83d0a2094dc8bd02526698f86b90"><span data-offset-key="4b9b83d0a2094dc8bd02526698f86b90:0">#</span></span></span></a><span data-key="b0bfcec1170247dea9167b7411ec6937"><span data-offset-key="b0bfcec1170247dea9167b7411ec6937:0">More resources</span></span>

<span data-key="847d9020a1df412bad81ed05e7c16750"><span data-offset-key="847d9020a1df412bad81ed05e7c16750:0">Explore snippet injection examples in our blog:</span></span>

-   

    <span data-key="1f0bd44993404a3aae0c9f9ef463f462"><span data-offset-key="1f0bd44993404a3aae0c9f9ef463f462:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://www.netlify.com/blog/2018/09/06/promoting-open-source-with-netlify-snippet-injection/" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="08d2669aee134d1fa52348aec8200534" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="80e28a32162343d8bb0c0e9752d0a82a"><span data-offset-key="80e28a32162343d8bb0c0e9752d0a82a:0">Promoting open source with Netlify snippet injection</span></span></span></a><span data-key="43666b4abf274be5b172f3bc0763b906"><span data-offset-key="43666b4abf274be5b172f3bc0763b906:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>

-   

    <span data-key="dd14358411f74bc0a6fbf0f505582fcf"><span data-offset-key="dd14358411f74bc0a6fbf0f505582fcf:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://www.netlify.com/blog/2020/12/14/add-web-monetization-to-your-sites-with-snippet-injection/" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="99cdef4ca1874132b7d0e19b95a75028" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="2b25b143daee4ea88cc4ea8b8f8fd4e9"><span data-offset-key="2b25b143daee4ea88cc4ea8b8f8fd4e9:0">Add web monetization to your sites with snippet injection</span></span></span></a><span data-key="f7cf1c793b6240a4bc7b5c58032d6199"><span data-offset-key="f7cf1c793b6240a4bc7b5c58032d6199:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>

<span data-key="007fbd1b28eb43abafa86050acf7b4f8"><span data-offset-key="007fbd1b28eb43abafa86050acf7b4f8:0">Prerendering</span></span>

<span data-key="cf322aef5cf9479d81414c1efd4be684">*This feature is in*<span data-offset-key="cf322aef5cf9479d81414c1efd4be684:1"> </span>`BETA`<span data-offset-key="cf322aef5cf9479d81414c1efd4be684:3">.</span></span>

<span data-key="10de4db4b3dc4c429c3d28822fc1fcba"><span data-offset-key="10de4db4b3dc4c429c3d28822fc1fcba:0">If you’re using a single-page app for a site that’s not behind a login, SEO is an important concern.</span></span>

<span data-key="8733d104cda846ef985131c13c0c9777"><span data-offset-key="8733d104cda846ef985131c13c0c9777:0">Google, Bing, Yandex and other search engines and crawlers support Google’s </span></span><a href="https://developers.google.com/webmasters/ajax-crawling/docs/specification" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="f99b122ec8ef4398a88b01cdece98252" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="3a66e271090648cf818f6714bdcfacbd"><span data-offset-key="3a66e271090648cf818f6714bdcfacbd:0">standard for Ajax Crawling</span></span></span></a><span data-key="a432621223464472993c117d5f28404e"><span data-offset-key="a432621223464472993c117d5f28404e:0">.</span></span>

<span data-key="87fc7665a0d94756ac8ad8627d5547b2"><span data-offset-key="87fc7665a0d94756ac8ad8627d5547b2:0">Normally Google will penalize sites heavily for using “cloaking”, meaning showing different content to Google than to normal web visitors, but for single page apps they have an exception. When detecting a single page app their crawler will send an </span>`_escaped_fragment_`<span data-offset-key="87fc7665a0d94756ac8ad8627d5547b2:2"> query parameter in the request, and the origin server can then choose to return a document that represents the content a user will actually get when the single page app is running.</span></span>

<span data-key="fef84b3a26fc4752a7cbef5c69bddc29"><span data-offset-key="fef84b3a26fc4752a7cbef5c69bddc29:0">Note</span></span>

<span data-key="636e5072a74440f38b228700dbeb29a3"><span data-offset-key="636e5072a74440f38b228700dbeb29a3:0">Google has marked their Standard for Ajax Crawling as deprecated. They’re still following the standard, but recommend that single page app authors just rely on Google’s built-in capacity for interpreting JavaScript applications. In our experience that’s often still not enough and prerendering is often still a necessity.</span></span>

<span data-key="d8c97b9f1290483a89214c3f2db38619"><span data-offset-key="d8c97b9f1290483a89214c3f2db38619:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://docs.netlify.com/site-deploys/post-processing/prerendering/#set-up-prerendering" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="503b6706bf7a4a919f5a09f36f465f05" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="c4e2772ddfad434287a88f2cb5741428"><span data-offset-key="c4e2772ddfad434287a88f2cb5741428:0">#</span></span></span></a><span data-key="caad4bd0edc249278e68443afa16949f"><span data-offset-key="caad4bd0edc249278e68443afa16949f:0">Set up prerendering</span></span>

<span data-key="b813fa0dfa2a4bc5a45fde710193412b"><span data-offset-key="b813fa0dfa2a4bc5a45fde710193412b:0">Netlify comes with built-in prerendering. You can enable it for your site at </span>**Site settings &gt; Build & deploy &gt; Post processing &gt; Prerendering**<span data-offset-key="b813fa0dfa2a4bc5a45fde710193412b:2">.</span></span>

<span data-key="137d31d2ca474d5499816e03fb76000c"><span data-offset-key="137d31d2ca474d5499816e03fb76000c:0">Enabling Netlify’s built-in prerendering</span></span>

<span data-key="b74e654558314931b10ce4def717e937"><span data-offset-key="b74e654558314931b10ce4def717e937:0">Our built-in prerendering service will cache prerendered pages for between 24 and 48 hours; this is not adjustable.</span></span>

### 

<span data-key="b36f620f64f0415aa2346505c3de9ede"><span data-offset-key="b36f620f64f0415aa2346505c3de9ede:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://docs.netlify.com/site-deploys/post-processing/prerendering/#external-services" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="faa7106c1d534a599fabf2fb696a6eb8" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="6b7bb7c0f0cc48a7a41d629123fc59fc"><span data-offset-key="6b7bb7c0f0cc48a7a41d629123fc59fc:0">#</span></span></span></a><span data-key="6eca4fd9539845ab8f9dcc976b8a4c99"><span data-offset-key="6eca4fd9539845ab8f9dcc976b8a4c99:0">External services</span></span>

<span data-key="b69cc9a47e6d47f69f5fd7894ffbda31">*This feature may not be available on all* </span><a href="https://www.netlify.com/pricing/" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="8076367de6dd4e349858c7d1ba7c189a" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="7027e7abf126403c8babe3664eba56cb"><em>plans</em></span></span></a><span data-key="538f953639e54f6f965e1bacb5e9789e">*.*</span>

<span data-key="ba01b579079d4e69bef9d81458836fbf"><span data-offset-key="ba01b579079d4e69bef9d81458836fbf:0">You can also use external services that can automate prerendering for you:</span></span>

-   

    <span data-key="b5ec5d5152f84f0197a20a5d88bdb341"><span data-offset-key="b5ec5d5152f84f0197a20a5d88bdb341:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://prerender.io/" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="b71896a35180496c8047011bb1ba5a72" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="e53973ed1da04361ace20eb9bc919127"><span data-offset-key="e53973ed1da04361ace20eb9bc919127:0">Prerender.io</span></span></span></a><span data-key="17e84a56e953462baf52764887e3f253"><span data-offset-key="17e84a56e953462baf52764887e3f253:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>

-   

    <span data-key="f8a455807eb04de7b6075be85cf98eac"><span data-offset-key="f8a455807eb04de7b6075be85cf98eac:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="http://www.brombone.com/" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="ee5f4ebb74464b29a9cae21066f5080f" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="539b83ea64094abfbf748883d7a71612"><span data-offset-key="539b83ea64094abfbf748883d7a71612:0">Brombone</span></span></span></a><span data-key="87273e73e1164655852d36b142df71d0"><span data-offset-key="87273e73e1164655852d36b142df71d0:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>

-   

    <span data-key="0880f8eb0fe74e6983db47b62de9b2e8"><span data-offset-key="0880f8eb0fe74e6983db47b62de9b2e8:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://prerender.cloud/" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="50299dff0bed4edd9a6d440bd1c51626" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="0ca2a0b6057e4128ac656cbd1d9e291c"><span data-offset-key="0ca2a0b6057e4128ac656cbd1d9e291c:0">Prerender.cloud</span></span></span></a><span data-key="851d1ec0411842a890d73ffd437c2ff9"><span data-offset-key="851d1ec0411842a890d73ffd437c2ff9:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>

<span data-key="996550a0872c42bbb9835cb45a5a3182"><span data-offset-key="996550a0872c42bbb9835cb45a5a3182:0">Prerender.io has an open-source version of their service that you can self-host.</span></span>

<span data-key="f06535fa015d4286b48e3e6537dc1d50"><span data-offset-key="f06535fa015d4286b48e3e6537dc1d50:0">If you want to use an external service, send us an email at </span></span><a href="https://bryan-guner.gitbook.io/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#e89b9d9898879a9ca8868d9c84818e91c68b8785" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="4eeeb8c3152d464283610930821f9eb4" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="8abac195c05e4736ad9cdc383970fd97"><span data-offset-key="8abac195c05e4736ad9cdc383970fd97:0"><span class="__cf_email__" data-cfemail="01727471716e7375416f64756d6867782f626e6c">[email protected]</span></span></span></span></a><span data-key="5cc168d9af954518bbe6c36db3cbd448"><span data-offset-key="5cc168d9af954518bbe6c36db3cbd448:0"> to let us know which service you’re using and its API token, and we’ll get you set up.</span></span>

<span data-key="f25bedd64d0a4b09a1fd25a0a88bc2f2"><span data-offset-key="f25bedd64d0a4b09a1fd25a0a88bc2f2:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://docs.netlify.com/site-deploys/post-processing/prerendering/#how-it-works" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="343b97f7b64e45b6879f10da64f7490f" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="d94bb51a018c48709f09346f33c8dc73"><span data-offset-key="d94bb51a018c48709f09346f33c8dc73:0">#</span></span></span></a><span data-key="22e08139eab34fc98903db36bf7125b2"><span data-offset-key="22e08139eab34fc98903db36bf7125b2:0">How it works</span></span>

<span data-key="65dd5e6129004fb1b3bc816f78b06ea0"><span data-offset-key="65dd5e6129004fb1b3bc816f78b06ea0:0">We’ve taken great care to implement support for prerendering in the most efficient manner possible.</span></span>

<span data-key="f155041c2ccb43189d402c6c16a8ca37"><span data-offset-key="f155041c2ccb43189d402c6c16a8ca37:0">When a request hits one of our CDN servers, our CDN software determines if it’s a prerendering request from a crawler. If prerendering is enabled for your site, our cache servers will contact the prerendering backend straight from our CDN nodes instead of serving the normal cached request.</span></span>

<span data-key="9bbbbff5b9674c05bca8ff10784ed680"><span data-offset-key="9bbbbff5b9674c05bca8ff10784ed680:0">If you’ve worked with Netlify support to configure an external service and the external prerendering backend makes good use of HTTP caching headers like max-age, ETags or Last-Modified dates, prerendered responses will be cached sensibly on our CDN edge nodes. In our initial tests we’ve seen average response times of ~100 ms to crawlers, which is low enough that Google will still give your site a SEO boost for being fast.</span></span>

<span data-key="5f666364166c4ef9bcb1027a85f0126e"><span data-offset-key="5f666364166c4ef9bcb1027a85f0126e:0">Visit our Support Forums to ask questions about </span></span><a href="https://answers.netlify.com/t/common-issue-understanding-and-debugging-prerendering/150/2" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="f53e91a0052c4998be903027997faa73" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="1061a4a2d89e45fea9f49f1692d974a2"><span data-offset-key="1061a4a2d89e45fea9f49f1692d974a2:0">understanding and debugging prerendering</span></span></span></a><span data-key="cd8d5b1fece84429a9864308bbfc5981"><span data-offset-key="cd8d5b1fece84429a9864308bbfc5981:0">.</span></span>

<span data-key="b4adc878d5794a88ae7704ec7f22229b"><span data-offset-key="b4adc878d5794a88ae7704ec7f22229b:0">Form detection</span></span>

<span data-key="c0bcf169e0e9429f8d034601b276487d"><span data-offset-key="c0bcf169e0e9429f8d034601b276487d:0">Netlify’s serverless form handling allows you to manage </span></span><a href="https://docs.netlify.com/forms/setup/" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="e521f149ffd04cb187bf5844655aa674" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="7914a29551a549b0a897b9fe1f2b71f5"><span data-offset-key="7914a29551a549b0a897b9fe1f2b71f5:0">forms</span></span></span></a><span data-key="e7c7282db88b4e0bbee90bd24a528c9f"><span data-offset-key="e7c7282db88b4e0bbee90bd24a528c9f:0"> without extra API calls or additional JavaScript. The built-in form detection feature allows our build bots to automatically parse your HTML at deploy time.</span></span>

<span data-key="fbd17294ef454266a95af0b7f8bb3e69"><span data-offset-key="fbd17294ef454266a95af0b7f8bb3e69:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://docs.netlify.com/site-deploys/post-processing/form-detection/#disable-form-detection" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="e5170237a5e54fe59425df2f59351f10" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="3f6ff9b437c046309397f6dbd9bfa8dc"><span data-offset-key="3f6ff9b437c046309397f6dbd9bfa8dc:0">#</span></span></span></a><span data-key="3527232fcdf2454f9da986d454dfa257"><span data-offset-key="3527232fcdf2454f9da986d454dfa257:0">Disable form detection</span></span>

<span data-key="99cc11c5705a43beb4f6d6487b2187c7"><span data-offset-key="99cc11c5705a43beb4f6d6487b2187c7:0">Although form detection is enabled by default, you may want to disable it if your site doesn’t have forms or you’re not using Netlify to manage them. Disabling form detection will reduce post processing and may speed up deploys.</span></span>

<span data-key="abc1b9a496bf4620b8456836ec1d2d16"><span data-offset-key="abc1b9a496bf4620b8456836ec1d2d16:0">To disable form detection for your site, go to </span>**Site settings &gt; Build & deploy &gt; Post processing &gt; Form detection**<span data-offset-key="abc1b9a496bf4620b8456836ec1d2d16:2">, and select </span>**Edit Settings**<span data-offset-key="abc1b9a496bf4620b8456836ec1d2d16:4">. Then clear the </span>**Run Form detection**<span data-offset-key="abc1b9a496bf4620b8456836ec1d2d16:6"> check box, and select </span>**Save**<span data-offset-key="abc1b9a496bf4620b8456836ec1d2d16:8">.</span></span>

<span data-key="f72cd37bc6d04fb9b89ca2630d8782dd"><span data-offset-key="f72cd37bc6d04fb9b89ca2630d8782dd:0">At your next site deploy, Netlify build bots will no longer parse new or updated HTML files for forms. </span></span><a href="https://docs.netlify.com/forms/submissions/#form-submissions-ui" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="59a033e956ef4c5f96939efa20cdaee7" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="a66ec692608340849b1b682f83d0636d"><span data-offset-key="a66ec692608340849b1b682f83d0636d:0">Form submission</span></span></span></a><span data-key="1872765959b44be18a65d41ae911ed66"><span data-offset-key="1872765959b44be18a65d41ae911ed66:0"> handling will be deactivated for any new or updated forms.</span></span>

<span data-key="7b19e3e5e6d440ab986786cc1c14f7c5"><span data-offset-key="7b19e3e5e6d440ab986786cc1c14f7c5:0">Warning</span></span>

<span data-key="dfcad17e9c424d64a42942f5c0d463ea"><span data-offset-key="dfcad17e9c424d64a42942f5c0d463ea:0">Disabling form detection is intended only for sites that don’t use Netlify Forms. If your site does use Netlify Forms, we recommend removing forms from your site code or altering your code to handle submissions by other means before disabling form detection.</span></span>

<span data-key="277220c8ecf448579894f879e8fce147"><span data-offset-key="277220c8ecf448579894f879e8fce147:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://docs.netlify.com/site-deploys/post-processing/form-detection/#re-enable-form-detection" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="20efe862e92f48928aa7cd4f1de33b7b" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="7467c6ae31d54b20914c85eea39685a2"><span data-offset-key="7467c6ae31d54b20914c85eea39685a2:0">#</span></span></span></a><span data-key="1c637d0c41ff445386200854bc70ada6"><span data-offset-key="1c637d0c41ff445386200854bc70ada6:0">Re-enable form detection</span></span>

<span data-key="ad07cb75bcf14d2885a489442472b9ba"><span data-offset-key="ad07cb75bcf14d2885a489442472b9ba:0">To enable form detection after disabling it, go to </span>**Site settings &gt; Build & deploy &gt; Post processing &gt; Form detection**<span data-offset-key="ad07cb75bcf14d2885a489442472b9ba:2">, and select </span>**Edit Settings**<span data-offset-key="ad07cb75bcf14d2885a489442472b9ba:4">. Then select </span>**Run Form detection**<span data-offset-key="ad07cb75bcf14d2885a489442472b9ba:6">, and select </span>**Save**<span data-offset-key="ad07cb75bcf14d2885a489442472b9ba:8">.</span></span>

<span data-key="180f21fb92fc4b9cb5a8f996d37be406"><span data-offset-key="180f21fb92fc4b9cb5a8f996d37be406:0">At your next site deploy, Netlify build bots will parse HTML to detect forms, and verified form submissions will be available on Netlify.</span></span>

<span data-key="ded196e336cb41be8219c98637459200"><span data-offset-key="ded196e336cb41be8219c98637459200:0">Configuration Options</span></span>

<span data-key="74b571f64a9c4174b0029233bf92c2e8"><span data-offset-key="74b571f64a9c4174b0029233bf92c2e8:0">Configuration File</span></span>

<span data-key="be122d773d5d43239b630d201a8a136e"><span data-offset-key="be122d773d5d43239b630d201a8a136e:0">All configuration options for Netlify CMS are specified in a </span>`config.yml`<span data-offset-key="be122d773d5d43239b630d201a8a136e:2"> file, in the folder where you access the editor UI (usually in the </span>`/admin`<span data-offset-key="be122d773d5d43239b630d201a8a136e:4"> folder).</span></span>

<span data-key="0a05e8d623814c989457225146dbf361"><span data-offset-key="0a05e8d623814c989457225146dbf361:0">Alternatively, you can specify a custom config file using a link tag:</span></span>

1

<span data-key="d6d20e91e6574261aaf985c0dc434ae3"><span data-offset-key="d6d20e91e6574261aaf985c0dc434ae3:0">&lt;!-- Note the "type" and "rel" attribute values, which are required. --&gt;</span></span>

2

<span data-key="10322180eefa4058b1145098e11aa452"><span data-offset-key="10322180eefa4058b1145098e11aa452:0">&lt;link href="path/to/config.yml" type="text/yaml" rel="cms-config-url"&gt;</span></span>

Copied!

<span data-key="b429aadbc37441649db5ca321e6a9183"><span data-offset-key="b429aadbc37441649db5ca321e6a9183:0">To see working configuration examples, you can </span></span><a href="https://www.netlifycms.org/docs/start-with-a-template" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="991ac09a08574e259431196b76bcdf53" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="6d24988c77d746f3bf778e6ceccd98d5"><span data-offset-key="6d24988c77d746f3bf778e6ceccd98d5:0">start from a template</span></span></span></a><span data-key="66bf358eaccd4a328309b044c4475d4a"><span data-offset-key="66bf358eaccd4a328309b044c4475d4a:0"> or check out the </span></span><a href="https://cms-demo.netlify.com/" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="107da603df3f49b6a183e34e4451d1a5" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="1396915484544650be9a6f5974dc622d"><span data-offset-key="1396915484544650be9a6f5974dc622d:0">CMS demo site</span></span></span></a><span data-key="ce24cc9b3b964b32a3c1f469fa928fe6"><span data-offset-key="ce24cc9b3b964b32a3c1f469fa928fe6:0">. (No login required: click the login button and the CMS will open.) You can refer to the demo </span></span><a href="https://github.com/netlify/netlify-cms/blob/master/dev-test/config.yml" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="6d402f5eb8e749eba780867212163d9a" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="bb84ba67e9f94606aebf517a05a76ce7"><span data-offset-key="bb84ba67e9f94606aebf517a05a76ce7:0">configuration code</span></span></span></a><span data-key="b7561d33697d474883b913b3e6cdad00"><span data-offset-key="b7561d33697d474883b913b3e6cdad00:0"> to see how each option was configured.</span></span>

<span data-key="2627ffa4124246fc800126e137d38d7c"><span data-offset-key="2627ffa4124246fc800126e137d38d7c:0">You can find details about all configuration options below. Note that </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/YAML#Basic_components" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="6ba8e1c3df8840d6bd1d213f192f8766" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="5e19cce0345d40f49e04ef532a186962"><span data-offset-key="5e19cce0345d40f49e04ef532a186962:0">YAML syntax</span></span></span></a><span data-key="aa75d9742cb44c69b9a92f79c91b3330"><span data-offset-key="aa75d9742cb44c69b9a92f79c91b3330:0"> allows lists and objects to be written in block or inline style, and the code samples below include a mix of both.</span></span>

<span data-key="671e16c32729498abc903e8d1d0ae021"><span data-offset-key="671e16c32729498abc903e8d1d0ae021:0">Backend</span></span>

<span data-key="efb25589306f4b03beee18e542e72fd8">*This setting is required.*</span>

<span data-key="52b18024083c445c80c11dbe979188a8"><span data-offset-key="52b18024083c445c80c11dbe979188a8:0">The </span>`backend`<span data-offset-key="52b18024083c445c80c11dbe979188a8:2"> option specifies how to access the content for your site, including authentication. Full details and code samples can be found in </span></span><a href="https://www.netlifycms.org/docs/backends-overview" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="fe315ee0483644ea95865fad29094dd0" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="df38a77d710e4ebab20c48db8fbd37c2"><span data-offset-key="df38a77d710e4ebab20c48db8fbd37c2:0">Backends</span></span></span></a><span data-key="6d8a82f356c644bcb6d4c156409d90a6"><span data-offset-key="6d8a82f356c644bcb6d4c156409d90a6:0">.</span></span>

<span data-key="c1a93496db4a4fe8b8d09d99b6d017cd">**Note**<span data-offset-key="c1a93496db4a4fe8b8d09d99b6d017cd:1">: no matter where you access Netlify CMS — whether running locally, in a staging environment, or in your published site — it will always fetch and commit files in your hosted repository (for example, on GitHub), on the branch you configured in your Netlify CMS config.yml file. This means that content fetched in the admin UI will match the content in the repository, which may be different from your locally running site. It also means that content saved using the admin UI will save directly to the hosted repository, even if you're running the UI locally or in staging.</span></span>

<span data-key="456523cd32e546d4b4633129436f925c"><span data-offset-key="456523cd32e546d4b4633129436f925c:0">Publish Mode</span></span>

<span data-key="07a9b8cc47294d869ff793367644b8de"><span data-offset-key="07a9b8cc47294d869ff793367644b8de:0">By default, all entries created or edited in the Netlify CMS are committed directly into the main repository branch.</span></span>

<span data-key="3309456dff3e4da398343499ccff64fe"><span data-offset-key="3309456dff3e4da398343499ccff64fe:0">The </span>`publish_mode`<span data-offset-key="3309456dff3e4da398343499ccff64fe:2"> option allows you to enable "Editorial Workflow" mode for more control over the content publishing phases. All unpublished entries will be arranged in a board according to their status, and they can be further reviewed and edited before going live.</span></span>

<span data-key="09f4c90b3e604cc597b7dd1f45c782f7">**Note:**<span data-offset-key="09f4c90b3e604cc597b7dd1f45c782f7:1"> Editorial workflow works with GitHub repositories, and support for GitLab and Bitbucket is </span></span><a href="https://www.netlifycms.org/docs/beta-features/#gitlab-and-bitbucket-editorial-workflow-support" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="b36e1412c6324b6fb0beb64dfb90739b" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-3187_262-3188-240__"><span data-key="901fd3b921444173961f3cd7bcc41b31"><span data-offset-key="901fd3b921444173961f3cd7bcc41b31:0">in beta</span></span></span></a><span data-key="446dee49add44fdd9142619af1881411"><span data-offset-key="446dee49add44fdd9142619af1881411:0">.</span></span>

<span data-key="65e699e8c64246bb844b09cfa7565d00"><span data-offset-key="65e699e8c64246bb844b09cfa7565d00:0">You can enable the Editorial Workflow with the following line in your Netlify CMS </span>`config.yml`<span data-offset-key="65e699e8c64246bb844b09cfa7565d00:2"> file:</span></span>

1

<span data-key="1b79df6bc65c43f6a837ec034a059dff"><span data-offset-key="1b79df6bc65c43f6a837ec034a059dff:0">\# /admin/config.yml</span></span>

2

<span data-key="2f1fbc9ad5864a2f909380ad11a5eb90"><span data-offset-key="2f1fbc9ad5864a2f909380ad11a5eb90:0">publish\_mode: editorial\_workflow</span></span>

Copied!

<span data-key="7aba2e2939d2409f9f817c4d5ae058b8"><span data-offset-key="7aba2e2939d2409f9f817c4d5ae058b8:0">From a technical perspective, the workflow translates editor UI actions into common Git commands:</span></span>

Actions in Netlify UI

Perform these Git actions

<span data-key="033d1cf6ebe744219dcef1d1463fbdaa"><span data-offset-key="033d1cf6ebe744219dcef1d1463fbdaa:0">Save draft</span></span>

<span data-key="c0c7f02f74404db29953815448de5330"><span data-offset-key="c0c7f02f74404db29953815448de5330:0">Commits to a new branch (named according to the pattern </span>`cms/collectionName/entrySlug`<span data-offset-key="c0c7f02f74404db29953815448de5330:2">), and opens a pull request</span></span>

<span data-key="5368b5ad321549529b41bd2256c22f72"><span data-offset-key="5368b5ad321549529b41bd2256c22f72:0">Edit draft</span></span>

<span data-key="864f633104904a65a19fbd7c3b0fac44"><span data-offset-key="864f633104904a65a19fbd7c3b0fac44:0">Pushes another commit to the draft branch/pull request</span></span>

<span data-key="896e52f7c9f34aaba5e67fa794c06759"><span data-offset-key="896e52f7c9f34aaba5e67fa794c06759:0">Approve and publish draft</span></span>

<span data-key="0b8d6b33dcab4bc7946f09482e1b79d5"><span data-offset-key="0b8d6b33dcab4bc7946f09482e1b79d5:0">Merges pull request and deletes branch</span></span>

<span data-key="d42e5d977f9146cba3d60c1a09b64ef1"><span data-offset-key="d42e5d977f9146cba3d60c1a09b64ef1:0">Media and Public Folders</span></span>

<span data-key="ad7f3f62a6244e129253ec4410643a2c"><span data-offset-key="ad7f3f62a6244e129253ec4410643a2c:0">Netlify CMS users can upload files to your repository using the Media Gallery. The following settings specify where these files are saved, and where they can be accessed on your built site.</span></span>

### 

<span data-key="4b364e8efb7b4da5bde288430beb6954"><span data-offset-key="4b364e8efb7b4da5bde288430beb6954:0">Media Folder</span></span>

<span data-key="d43551e56d55405993c4643229dcd839">*This setting is required.*</span>

<span data-key="b47c9c8b03dd43828d68fbf29236e4e4"><span data-offset-key="b47c9c8b03dd43828d68fbf29236e4e4:0">The </span>`media_folder`<span data-offset-key="b47c9c8b03dd43828d68fbf29236e4e4:2"> option specifies the folder path where uploaded files should be saved, relative to the base of the repo.</span></span>

1

<span data-key="38fab067ba644d59889e4a91057f1cb6"><span data-offset-key="38fab067ba644d59889e4a91057f1cb6:0">media\_folder: "static/images/uploads"</span></span>

Copied!

### 

<span data-key="70168061371e4a2c997ea908c7947a74"><span data-offset-key="70168061371e4a2c997ea908c7947a74:0">Public Folder</span></span>

<span data-key="9eaeb42d6de2445da23d0f0ee5c152f2"><span data-offset-key="9eaeb42d6de2445da23d0f0ee5c152f2:0">The </span>`public_folder`<span data-offset-key="9eaeb42d6de2445da23d0f0ee5c152f2:2"> option specifies the folder path where the files uploaded by the media library will be accessed, relative to the base of the built site. For fields controlled by \[file\] or \[image\] widgets, the value of the field is generated by prepending this path to the filename of the selected file. Defaults to the value of </span>`media_folder`<span data-offset-key="9eaeb42d6de2445da23d0f0ee5c152f2:4">, with an opening </span>`/`<span data-offset-key="9eaeb42d6de2445da23d0f0ee5c152f2:6"> if one is not already included.</span></span>

1

<span data-key="52b9a1c9067e40cf9e4c354ac1dc1708"><span data-offset-key="52b9a1c9067e40cf9e4c354ac1dc1708:0">public\_folder: "/images/uploads"</span></span>

Copied!

<span data-key="e271e46d86924d8fa860450ecdf5abe6"><span data-offset-key="e271e46d86924d8fa860450ecdf5abe6:0">Based on the settings above, if a user used an image widget field called </span>`avatar`<span data-offset-key="e271e46d86924d8fa860450ecdf5abe6:2"> to upload and select an image called </span>`philosoraptor.png`<span data-offset-key="e271e46d86924d8fa860450ecdf5abe6:4">, the image would be saved to the repository at </span>`/static/images/uploads/philosoraptor.png`<span data-offset-key="e271e46d86924d8fa860450ecdf5abe6:6">, and the </span>`avatar`<span data-offset-key="e271e46d86924d8fa860450ecdf5abe6:8"> field for the file would be set to </span>`/images/uploads/philosoraptor.png`<span data-offset-key="e271e46d86924d8fa860450ecdf5abe6:10">.</span></span>

<span data-key="1fff3c1c70f14d998ae8c304f869fe75"><span data-offset-key="1fff3c1c70f14d998ae8c304f869fe75:0">This setting can be set to an absolute URL e.g. </span>`https://netlify.com/media`<span data-offset-key="1fff3c1c70f14d998ae8c304f869fe75:2"> should you wish, however in general this is not advisable as content should have relative paths to other content.</span></span>

<span data-key="8e0c114af96047c19d0d43e42816327a"><span data-offset-key="8e0c114af96047c19d0d43e42816327a:0">Media Library</span></span>

<span data-key="4509a2f201b449a6b8c90578855b4fec"><span data-offset-key="4509a2f201b449a6b8c90578855b4fec:0">Media library integrations are configured via the </span>`media_library`<span data-offset-key="4509a2f201b449a6b8c90578855b4fec:2"> property, and its value should be an object with at least a </span>`name`<span data-offset-key="4509a2f201b449a6b8c90578855b4fec:4"> property. A </span>`config`<span data-offset-key="4509a2f201b449a6b8c90578855b4fec:6"> property can also be used for options that should be passed to the library in use.</span></span>

<span data-key="808cde624ded48d7ba6f7ab9982848b7">**Example:**</span>

1

<span data-key="bca2ddc37608470097fe430a70b00dd5"><span data-offset-key="bca2ddc37608470097fe430a70b00dd5:0">media\_library:</span></span>

2

<span data-key="e2f548472b514ed884ddff99cf8cee1e"><span data-offset-key="e2f548472b514ed884ddff99cf8cee1e:0"> name: uploadcare</span></span>

3

<span data-key="7dab84d42b7b4ae9984b1e13721b6061"><span data-offset-key="7dab84d42b7b4ae9984b1e13721b6061:0"> config:</span></span>

4

<span data-key="33933fbf24b046d1978cae5eee5e3cfd"><span data-offset-key="33933fbf24b046d1978cae5eee5e3cfd:0"> publicKey: demopublickey</span></span>

Copied!

<span data-key="634ebc1f8c0444ac8a36658d67b0b489"><span data-offset-key="634ebc1f8c0444ac8a36658d67b0b489:0">Site URL</span></span>

<span data-key="d3cec8f63eda45319c56995188611dda"><span data-offset-key="d3cec8f63eda45319c56995188611dda:0">The </span>`site_url`<span data-offset-key="d3cec8f63eda45319c56995188611dda:2"> setting should provide a URL to your published site. May be used by the CMS for various functionality. Used together with a collection's </span>`preview_path`<span data-offset-key="d3cec8f63eda45319c56995188611dda:4"> to create links to live content.</span></span>

<span data-key="0a6027c77928471db6c9ed71d33308ab">**Example:**</span>

1

<span data-key="8510d484b1b84668a0afd54c1bb698a1"><span data-offset-key="8510d484b1b84668a0afd54c1bb698a1:0">site\_url: https://your-site.com</span></span>

Copied!

<span data-key="431eef1ea47946a3b62e82992530f681"><span data-offset-key="431eef1ea47946a3b62e82992530f681:0">Display URL</span></span>

<span data-key="6be334c2a1f44146accfa4c2149188ba"><span data-offset-key="6be334c2a1f44146accfa4c2149188ba:0">When the </span>`display_url`<span data-offset-key="6be334c2a1f44146accfa4c2149188ba:2"> setting is specified, the CMS UI will include a link in the fixed area at the top of the page, allowing content authors to easily return to your main site. The text of the link consists of the URL without the protocol portion (e.g., </span>`your-site.com`<span data-offset-key="6be334c2a1f44146accfa4c2149188ba:4">).</span></span>

<span data-key="a1e353ed86bf498e878d70f05b6bf916"><span data-offset-key="a1e353ed86bf498e878d70f05b6bf916:0">Defaults to </span>`site_url`<span data-offset-key="a1e353ed86bf498e878d70f05b6bf916:2">.</span></span>

<span data-key="742be0516a3e48d4b8e4b772fea3da30">**Example:**</span>

1

<span data-key="e0add46652234367a4e7c37b8abcc351"><span data-offset-key="e0add46652234367a4e7c37b8abcc351:0">display\_url: https://your-site.com</span></span>

Copied!

<span data-key="c37d8a98a1934661ab6ded386799f823"><span data-offset-key="c37d8a98a1934661ab6ded386799f823:0">Custom Logo</span></span>

<span data-key="852ae037d843407488b7504d124bacb6"><span data-offset-key="852ae037d843407488b7504d124bacb6:0">When the </span>`logo_url`<span data-offset-key="852ae037d843407488b7504d124bacb6:2"> setting is specified, the CMS UI will change the logo displayed at the top of the login page, allowing you to brand the CMS with your own logo. </span>`logo_url`<span data-offset-key="852ae037d843407488b7504d124bacb6:4"> is assumed to be a URL to an image file.</span></span>

<span data-key="8a3ebf3cd2724dba97f902f55714c5d5">**Example:**</span>

1
